  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6c90caec-8d83-4218-bf4e-28b603a4e8f9'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer16689663939078709291">Drew Evans is a winner. Handsome and arrogant, he makes multimillion dollar business deals and seduces New York’s most beautiful women with just a smile. He has loyal friends and an indulgent family.   <span id="freeText16689663939078709291" style="display:none">Drew Evans is a winner. Handsome and arrogant, he makes multimillion dollar business deals and seduces New York’s most beautiful women with just a smile. He has loyal friends and an indulgent family. So why has he been shuttered in his apartment for seven days, miserable and depressed? <br /><br />He’ll tell you he has the flu.<br /><br />But we all know that’s not really true.<br /><br />Katherine Brooks is brilliant, beautiful and ambitious. She refuses to let anything - or anyone - derail her path to success. When Kate is hired as the new associate at Drew’s father’s investment banking firm, every aspect of the dashing playboy’s life is thrown into a tailspin. The professional competition she brings is unnerving, his attraction to her is distracting, his failure to entice her into his bed is exasperating. <br /><br />Then, just when Drew is on the cusp of having everything he wants, his overblown confidence threatens to ruin it all. Will he be able untangle his feelings of lust and tenderness, frustration and fulfillment? Will he rise to the most important challenge of his life? <br /><br />Can Drew Evans win at love? <br /><br />Tangled is not your mother’s romance novel. It is an outrageous, passionate, witty narrative about a man who knows a lot about women…just not as much as he thinks he knows. As he tells his story, Drew learns the one thing he never wanted in life, is the only thing he can’t live without.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16689663939078709291" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_608108566" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/608108566" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608108566?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608108566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3573567270710367833"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420508i/834139._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> Hilarious, romantic, all-out FUN!! <br/><br/>Think Wallbanger meets Beautiful Bastard :)<br/><br/>You smiling yet? </b><br/><br/>I was hooked from the first line and smiling wide by the end of the first page. If you are a fan of enemies-to-lovers stories, you will LOVE Tangled!<br/><br/>I swear half my book is highlighted. I laughed out loud, grinned till my cheeks ached and just generally loved it!<br/><br/>The story is about Drew. In real life, Drew is a clean-shaven, well-groomed, expensive suit wearing professional. But, at the start of the st</span>
  <span id="freeText3573567270710367833" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420508i/834139._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Hilarious, romantic, all-out FUN!! <br><br>Think Wallbanger meets Beautiful Bastard :)<br><br>You smiling yet? </b><br><br>I was hooked from the first line and smiling wide by the end of the first page. If you are a fan of enemies-to-lovers stories, you will LOVE Tangled!<br><br>I swear half my book is highlighted. I laughed out loud, grinned till my cheeks ached and just generally loved it!<br><br>The story is about Drew. In real life, Drew is a clean-shaven, well-groomed, expensive suit wearing professional. But, at the start of the story, he’s a miserable un-showered, un-shaven heap locked in a messy apartment overflowing with old pizza boxes while claiming to have the flu.<br><br>Right.<br><br>What he really has is a bad case of the Break Up.<br><br>See Real Life Drew was once a player. Why settle for one when there were so many willing ones tripping over themselves to be with him?<br><br>“I’ve never seduced a woman before.<br>Shocking, I know.<br>Let me clarify. I’ve never had to seduce a woman before, not in the typical sense. Usually it just takes a look, a wink, a smile. A friendly greeting, maybe a drink or two. After that, the only verbal exchange involves short, one-word phrases like harder, more, lower… You get the point.”  <br>But he’s fallen in love. Finally. Problem is, she’s getting married… to someone else. Hence the miserable, moping, un-shaved heap. This is his story.<br><br>It starts off going back in time to when they first met. Drew meets Kate at a club one night and, despite the flirting, she walks away. When Kate gets hired by his office, it puts him in a frustrating situation because office romances are on his no-no list.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Kate Brooks is officially scratched off my list of potentials. She is forbidden, untouchable, a no-way-never. Right next to my friends’ ex-girlfriends, the boss’ daughter, and my sister’s best friends.<br>Well, that last category is a bit of a gray area.” </i> </blockquote><br>We are told the story by Drew. He can be a bit of an asshat but you really just can’t help falling for him – he’s that lovable. He both narrates the events and breaks the 4th wall by talking directly to us as the reader. It’s totally awesome! It’s like he’s right there telling you the story. There are times when his commentary on what was going on just had me in stitches. Here’s a random quote:<br><br><blockquote> <i> “Once again, to the ladies out there — here’s a fact for you: Men pretty much have sex on the brain twenty-four-seven. The exact figure is like every 5.2 seconds or some shit like that.<br><br>The point is, when you ask, “What do you want for dinner?” we’re thinking about screwing you on the kitchen counter. When you’re telling us about the sappy film you watched with your girlfriends last week, we’re thinking about the porno we saw on cable last night. When you show us the designer shoes you bought on sale, we’re thinking how nice they would look on our shoulders.<br><br>I just thought you’d want to know. Don’t shoot the messenger.” </i> </blockquote><br>And if you like strong heroines, you will LOVE Kate. She is smart, confident, sassy and absolutely determined not to become another notch on Drew’s bed post. She has plans, dreams, goals and no time for a playboy.<br><br><blockquote> <i> “If we’re going to work together, Drew, I think we’re should get a few things straight. I’m not your sweetheart. My name is Kate — Katherine. Use it. And I’m not a kiss-ass. I don’t have to be. My work speaks for itself.” </i> </blockquote><br>Their banter and ‘sparring’ was just priceless! Tangled was essentially an enemies-to-lovers story about guy falling in love for the first time with a girl who goes toe-to-toe with him on everything. I loved watching them work through their issues. And when Drew finally decides to fight for Kate’s heart, the lengths to which he goes are just laugh-out-loud awesome!<br><br><blockquote> <i> “It makes me want to kiss her and strangle her at the same time. I’ve never been into S&amp;M, but I’m beginning to see its benefits.” </i> </blockquote><br>The book wasn’t always funny per say, but the whole mood was light hearted. The sex was hot, the characters were lovable, the writing was witty and it has a happy ending :)<br><br>If you are looking for a FUN read, this is it!!!!<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><i> Thank you to the publisher for providing me an ARC to review. </i><br><br>******************************<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363075752l/16073738.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BLURB --&gt; <i> Drew Evans is a winner. Handsome and arrogant, he makes multimillion dollar business deals and seduces New York’s most beautiful women with just a smile. He has loyal friends and an indulgent family. So why has he been shuttered in his apartment for seven days, miserable and depressed? <br><br>He’ll tell you he has the flu.<br><br>But we all know that’s not really true.<br><br>Katherine Brooks is brilliant, beautiful and ambitious. She refuses to let anything - or anyone - derail her path to success. When Kate is hired as the new associate at Drew’s father’s investment banking firm, every aspect of the dashing playboy’s life is thrown into a tailspin. The professional competition she brings is unnerving, his attraction to her is distracting, his failure to entice her into his bed is exasperating. <br><br>Then, just when Drew is on the cusp of having everything he wants, his overblown confidence threatens to ruin it all. Will he be able untangle his feelings of lust and tenderness, frustration and fulfillment? Will he rise to the most important challenge of his life? <br><br>Can Drew Evans win at love? <br><br>Tangled is not your mother’s romance novel. It is an outrageous, passionate, witty narrative about a man who knows a lot about women…just not as much as he thinks he knows. As he tells his story, Drew learns the one thing he never wanted in life, is the only thing he can’t live without.<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3573567270710367833" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Baba  " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669232-baba"><img alt="Baba  " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564910043p2/4669232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Baba  " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Baba  " href="/user/show/4669232-baba">Baba  </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=humor">humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved">books-kelly-and-baba-liked-or-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669232-baba?shelf=five-star-reads">five-star-reads</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer621049551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16807407224422449710"><b>5 stars.*****Review completed May 24, 2013</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/660094.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mn0zhxlpPy1qffcrao3_500_zps6ad39d04.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Fuck, yeah. That’s good. Yeah, like that.“<br/>See that guy—black suit, devilishly handsome? Yeah, the guy getting the blow job from the luscious redhead in the bathroom stall? That’s me. The real me. MBF: Me Before Flu.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840390.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mn0zhxlpPy1qffcrao6_250_zps4c3f10ce.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>So, like I said what you’re seeing right now isn’t the real me. I have the flu.<br/>Influenza.<br/>Have you ever noticed some of the worst sicknesses in history have a lyrical sound to them? Words like malaria, diarrhea, cholera. Do</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16807407224422449710" style="display:none"><b>5 stars.*****Review completed May 24, 2013</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/660094.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mn0zhxlpPy1qffcrao3_500_zps6ad39d04.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Fuck, yeah. That’s good. Yeah, like that.“<br>See that guy—black suit, devilishly handsome? Yeah, the guy getting the blow job from the luscious redhead in the bathroom stall? That’s me. The real me. MBF: Me Before Flu.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840390.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mn0zhxlpPy1qffcrao6_250_zps4c3f10ce.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>So, like I said what you’re seeing right now isn’t the real me. I have the flu.<br>Influenza.<br>Have you ever noticed some of the worst sicknesses in history have a lyrical sound to them? Words like malaria, diarrhea, cholera. Do you think they do that on purpose? To make it a nice way to say you feel like something that dropped out of your dog’s ass?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Poor Drew. He looks like a zombie when he's got the flu. *pets* *evil grin*<br>Isn't it strange that every man who's got the flu is dying--right in front of your eyes. A sick man is always moaning a woman's ears off. Terrible.<br>Reminds me of my two little guys and my ex…all their antics…tsk-tsk...<br>My mom told me once that if men would bear kids, then the couples would never have more than one child. Men couldn't withstand the pain, they would cave in after the first delivery.<br><br>I apologize in advance for adding too many quotes and for getting a tiny bit long-winded. There's something you need to know, though. Drew is the perfect man-whore and Baba is the perfect quotes-whore. Ramps up the fun factor, it's all good. *cough*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840391.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mmx3pwrZND1qmf14oo1_500_zpsf65e1576.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>But I have rules—standards, you might say. One of them is no screwing around at the office. I don’t shit where I eat, I don’t fuck where I work. Never mind the sexual harassment issues it would bring up;  it’s just not good business. It’s unprofessional.<br> <br>And she works here. In my office, where I have sworn to never…ever…screw around. Her warm, soft hand slides perfectly into mine, and two thoughts enter my head simultaneously.<br>The first is: God hates me.  The second is: I have been a naughty, naughty boy for most of my life, and this is my payback. And you know what they say about payback, right?<br>Yep. She’s one hairy bitch.<br> <br>“Well, you could do the noble thing and bow out.” Yeah—like that’ll happen.<br>“In your dreams.”<br>I smirk. „Actually my dreams involve you bending over something…not bowing.”<br>She makes a disgusted sound. “Could you be any more of a pig?”<br>“I was kidding. Why do you have to be so fucking serious all the time? You should learn how to take a joke.”<br>“I can take a joke,” she tells me, sounding insulted.<br>“Yeah? When?”<br>“When it’s not being delivered by a childish jackass who thinks he’s God’s gift to women.”<br>“I am not childish.”<br>God’s gift on the other hand?  My record speaks for itself.<br>“Oh, bite me.”<br>I wish.<br>„Nice comeback, Kate. Very mature.“<br>“You’re a jerk.“<br>„You’re a…an Alexandra.”<br>She pauses a second and looks at me blankly.<br>“What the hell does that even mean?”<br>Think about it. It will come to you.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840392.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m54bnw6sR51qj73e2o1_500_zpsef022de1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Kate walks into her office and closes the door, leaving me standing on the outside. This is where men got the shitty end of the stick, people. When God gave Eve that extra rib? He should have given us something extra too. Like mental telepathy.<br>I once heard my mother tell my father that she shouldn’t have to explain why she was pissed.  That if he didn’t already know what he’d done wrong, then he wasn’t really sorry for it. What the fuck does that even mean? Newsflash, ladies:  We can’t read your thoughts. And frankly, I’m not entirely sure I’d want to. The female mind is a scary place to be.<br> <br>Oh yeah. Just one more little detail you should know: I haven’t gotten laid in twelve days.<br>Twelve days.<br>Two hundred and eighty-eight sex-free hours. I can’t calculate the minutes—it’s too depressing. Remember all work and no play makes Drew a cranky boy? Well, at this point, Drew is practically a goddamned psychopath, okay?<br> <br>Because you know how some people have gay-dar? Well, I have dump-dar. That means I can pick out a recently dumped female a mile away. They’re easy pickings. All you have to tell them is that their ex is an idiot for letting them go, and they’ll be begging you to nail them.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kate <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> now falls into the aforementioned dumped category. Should be a sure thing, right?</i>

</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840393.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mlvm2f4RbN1s9b724o5_500_zpsa4e6b6ac.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

    <b>Just so you know, men don’t expect a woman to smell like Winter Pine or Niagara Falls or whatever the fuck those feminine products say. It’s a pussy—it’s supposed to smell like one. That’s the fucking turn on.<br> <br>I read an article once that said having sex extends the human life span. At this rate, Kate and I are going to live forever. I’ve lost count of the number of times we’ve done it. It’s like a mosquito bite—the more you scratch, the more it itches.<br>I’m just glad I bought the extra-large box of condoms at Costco.</b>

</blockquote><br><br>The man on woman action was hot and left Drew somewhat disheveled...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840394.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mn0zhxlpPy1qffcrao8_250_zpsc2aaa2de.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840395.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mbnuj99bRi1rrl2a0o1_500_zpsf7f999af.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The infamous Bad Word Jar…she's going to rob you blind, Drew. *smirk*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422407i/840396.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-05-23um115220_zps5308719c.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew and his niece Mackenzie are so, so adorable together! Loved their interaction. CUTE. The man would do anything for that girl.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422407i/840397.jpg" alt=" photo 1ee9c865-8512-43f0-adc0-f5b16a7c5cba_zps996a3d4f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The next part is spoiler-tagged in order to shorten my review. Just go ahead and read it, it won't spoil it for you. :-)<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"Yes, I wanted Mackenzie to meet Kate. I didn't want you meeting Kate until I was done smoothing things the hell over."<br>Mackenzie takes my friend the Bad Word Jar out of her backpack and holds it up. I put two dollars in.<br>She sticks her face in the mouth of the jar and looks up at me with a frown. "Um…Uncle Drew? Bad words no cost one dollar no more. They cost ten."<br>"Ten? Since when?"<br>She's excited. "It was Kate's idea. She say the maconomy is bad."<br>What the hell is maconomy? (Drew, Drew…tsk-tsk…I thought you were so smart?)<br>"She call it in…in…"<br>"Inflation." Alexandra finishes with a smile.<br>"Yeah, that."<br>Inflation.<br>Great.<br>Thanks, Kate.<br>I raise my brows at Mackenzie. "Do you take American Express?" She giggles. I pay my fine in cash. "How about you add up the rest on your calculator, honey?"<br>She's going to need it. I have a feeling this little discussion is going to put me in the triple digits.<br><br><br>"Sweetheart," I say, "you did Uncle Drew a huge favor. Anything you want for Christmas--name it and it's yours. And I mean anything."<br>Her eyes widen at the possibilities. She glances at my sister and then whispers conspiratorially, "Can I have a pony?"<br>Oh, boy.<br>I think about it for exactly one second.<br>"Absolutely."<br>She squeezes me tighter and squeals.<br>"Only…don't tell mommy until after it's delivered, okay?"<br>I may have to enter the witness protection program after this one.</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><b>I friggin' loved it! <i>Tangled</i> was pure fun, fun, fun! You don't believe me? Seriously? You are missing out on a real winner.</b><br><br><br><br>Dear Drew,<br><br>Nice to meet you, darling. Um…I'm in awe. Honestly, I'm kinda speechless and I swear to you that happens not all the time. I'm sitting in front of my laptop, and I'm not sure how to review your story. I might as well do it short and sweet, right? No, you pervert, I didn't say I might as well do you. *stern look* Rein in your overly imaginative thoughts. Do some yoga, that should do the trick. See? That's more like it. By the way, did you know that yoga improves your sex life? Check this out:<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.psychologytoday.com/blog/all-about-sex/201007/want-better-sex-do-yoga">http://www.psychologytoday.com/blog/a...</a><br><br>Come to think of it, I'm not sure if you would survive even better sex coz your current sex life seems to be quite chirpy, and Kate is wearing you the f@ck out. You shouldn't disturb me since I'm working on my review. I mean I need to focus on the heart of the matter, right? Hence, you wouldn't want me to screw it up. *a look of utter exasperation* Note to readers: Have you seen how exasperating and tenacious that man is? Whatever. Let's get down to business…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Did you know that if you put a frog in boiling water, he'll jump out? But, if you put one in cold water and heat it slowly, he'll stay in. And boil to death. He won't even try to get out. He won't even know he's dying. Until it's too late.<br>Men are a lot like frogs.<br><br>If, by some catastrophe, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kate won't take me back, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I might as well shave my head and move to frigging Tibet. I hear the monks are hiring.</b>

</blockquote><br><br>Yeah, Drew, you are something else. Calling you arrogant with a supremely inflated libido doesn't even begin to cover it. Hmm…please spare me your 'widening' eyes right now coz it's such a cliché in romance books. Frankly, it annoys the f@ck out of me and we're back to real life, aren't we? I do not need that crap. Thank you for being so forthcoming. *mwah* Huh? Did you just blush? Where was I? Oh, back to your story…<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You have no idea how important regular sexual gratification is for us. It's crucial. Vital.<br>I'll explain.<br>In 2004, UCLA conducted a survey to determine how highly women valued getting off in relation to other daily activities. You know what they found? Eight in ten--that's eighty percent--said if given the choice between sex or sleep, they would choose sleep.<br>In that same year, NYU conducted its own study. With rats. They implanted electrodes in the brains of male rats and put two buttons in their cages. When the lucky little bastards pushed the blue button, the electrodes triggered an orgasm. When they pushed a red button, they were given food.<br>Care to guess what happened to all the rats?<br>They died.<br>They f@cking starved to death.<br>They never pushed the red button.<br>Need I say more?<br>Anyway, here I am. Stuck in my own little cage with no goddamn blue button. But…</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Dude, I need to tell you that you've got one seriously warped mind. I'm not sure but have you seen a doctor recently? I mean it, man, since your brain seems to suffer from a serious overload of Ecstasy or cocaine. I actually thought that you could swallow a couple Valium. Um…you see I thought it could help you to ramp down your overactive mind. Honestly, what man's mind is working 24/7? What man is thinking all the freakin' time? What man is talking all the time? Does your dirty mind ever sleep? Gawd, doesn't it wear you out? Truth be told, that man doesn't exist. Hey, calm down, ok? Alrighty, I'll take it back. *goes on knees* There is the one and only Drew Evans! <i>The</i> man. The star. God's <s>redundant</s> gift to women. *gasp* I cannot believe I just said <i>that.</i> Yeah, yeah, spare me your smug smile, dude. I know you are enjoying yourself immensely. *huffs*<br><br>Would you please do me a favor? Tell your author that I loved her sense of humor. I loved her writing and it was an incredibly hilarious trip. I totally enjoyed being in your naughty little mind and writing <i>Tangled</i> in first person present tense from your POV was a real knockout. See? Here comes the much awaited praise from moi! Also, I really appreciated her choice of secondary characters. They were well drawn and added to the fun factor, for sure. Your interaction with Mackenzie was utterly priceless. <b>
  <i>Bagina,</i>
</b> anyone? Well, all the power to the vaginas, I am <i>so</i> with you. You sure are an enlightened man, Drew. *grin* <i>Tangled</i> is actually a breath of fresh air among too many mediocre contemporary romance books.<br><br>I must admit, however, that I couldn't take you overly serious. Your character seemed to be kinda exaggerated, something like a parody, you know? Don't get me wrong. I loved it nonetheless, and many things you said were true. Seriously, I loved every single pearl of wisdom that came out of your <s>crude</s> delicious mouth. Well, I know you want me to get down and dirty now. Hah! I know you are waiting for me to hail you with praise for your sexual prowess. Yes, yes, yes, you can eat me all night long, ok? I mean what does it cost me to admit it, right? But you did it and I can't tell you how proud I am of you. Do you remember when you were talking about the best fu@@ing advice ever? <i>Assume nothing. Even if you think you know everything. Even if you're sure that you're right. Get confirmation.</i> Yes! *high five* You have learned your lesson, Drew. Besides, do you remember what else you told me? Yup. This <i>relationship shit</i> is exhausting. Then again you must admit it's so damn worth it, isn't it?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422407i/840398.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-05-23um133756_zps7a6df290.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew, darling, I need to come to an end now. You know I feel a little bit worn out; I'm not getting any younger either. Besides, my life is kinda busy. Though it was nice chatting with you, and I hope to see you around.<br><br>I wish you a life full of love, laughter and happiness.<br><br>All the best and take care.<br><br>Baba xxx<br><br><br><br><br>I have been laughing my ass off all the time. <i>Tangled</i> gets the <i>
  <b>Babalicious Stamp of Approval.</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422407ra/840399.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mmut6d4AXq1rj4uo2o1_500_zps9405422a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Pussy whipped, thy name is Drew.<br>Yeah, I know. It's okay. I don't mind. 'Cause if this is the Dark Side? Sign me up. Seriously. Don't be surprised if I start skipping down the street singing, "Zip-a-Dee-fucking-Doo-Dah." I'm that happy.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I don't mind either. Sign me up. I'm happy. Seriously. Cannot wait to read the next book in the series!<br><br><br><b>P.S.</b> Drew, dearie, just so know…the NILF comment was crude. *shakes head disapprovingly*<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer620742815" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7234272615444076088"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg' width='200' height='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>*1.5 stars*<br/><br/>Okay, I know that everyone loves this book. But, honestly, <b>I <i>despised</i> it.</b><br/><br/>This book sort of reminded me of a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley' title='Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley</a> book. There was this stereotype of what a "guy" is, and how a "guy" thinks. <br/><br/>But...<br/><br/>I've known a guy or two in my day. This book reads like what a GIRL thinks a guy is like. <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_' title='Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tangled</a> had so many loathsome tropes. We get a <b>magical vagina</b> turning a pigheaded guy into a devoted man. We get the <b>adorable niece</b> (which can be replaced by doting younger sister in some books</span>
  <span id="freeText7234272615444076088" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1472750173i/20237706._SX540_.jpg" width="200" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>*1.5 stars*<br><br>Okay, I know that everyone loves this book. But, honestly, <b>I <i>despised</i> it.</b><br><br>This book sort of reminded me of a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> book. There was this stereotype of what a "guy" is, and how a "guy" thinks. <br><br>But...<br><br>I've known a guy or two in my day. This book reads like what a GIRL thinks a guy is like. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_" title="Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a> had so many loathsome tropes. We get a <b>magical vagina</b> turning a pigheaded guy into a devoted man. We get the <b>adorable niece</b> (which can be replaced by doting younger sister in some books), who shows a dickhead's "loving" side. We get <b>blatant misogyny and even SEXUAL HARRASMENT at work</b> framed as "just teasing" and "all in good fun," offset by, of course, an even bigger asshole who "crosses the line" and shows that the MC isn't all that bad. <br><br><b>The male MC doesn't respect the female MC.</b> He doesn't respect her boundaries, he doesn't respect her intelligence, and he doesn't show that he is worthy of her for a hot second. <br><br><b>I didn't think this book was funny. I didn't think this book was entertaining. I didn't think the male MC read like a man or how a man thinks. </b><br><br>The only reason this book gets an extra 1/2 a star is because the narrator did a nice job reading the story, but if I didn't spend good money on the ebook + the audiobook upgrade, I would have DNFed it (like I wanted to do!) ages ago. <br><br>No offense to my dozens of friends who loved this one, but the sooner I forget this book, the better.</span>

<div id="review_608288360" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/608288360" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608288360?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608288360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10112786373374264259"><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834270.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>FUN STORYLINE + HILARIOUS DIALOGUE + HOT HERO & KICKASS HEROINE = 5 STAR WORTHY WINNING COMBINATION.</b><br/><br/>And reading this story from the point of view of a guy like Drew?<b> Pure fun and entertainment</b>, I assure you! ;)<br/></p><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834271.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Let's meet the man of the hour shall we...<br/><br/></p><blockquote>
  <b>"See that guy - black suit, devilishly handsome? The guy getting the blow job from the luscious redhead in the bathroom stall? That's me. The <i>real</i> me. MBF: Me Before Flu."</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Yep, we're talking about no one other than the real <b>Drew Evans --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420533i/834272._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He's the</span>
  <span id="freeText10112786373374264259" style="display:none"><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834270.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FUN STORYLINE + HILARIOUS DIALOGUE + HOT HERO &amp; KICKASS HEROINE = 5 STAR WORTHY WINNING COMBINATION.</b><br><br>And reading this story from the point of view of a guy like Drew?<b> Pure fun and entertainment</b>, I assure you! ;)<br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834271.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's meet the man of the hour shall we...<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>"See that guy - black suit, devilishly handsome? The guy getting the blow job from the luscious redhead in the bathroom stall? That's me. The <i>real</i> me. MBF: Me Before Flu."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Yep, we're talking about no one other than the real <b>Drew Evans --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420533i/834272._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's the kind of guy who's used to <i>always</i> getting what he wants. He's the kind of guy who <i>"never rides the same roller coaster twice"</i>. But now? Things have changed... He'll tell you he has the flu, but what really happened? Well, that's an entirely different story... One you're about to hear, the uncensored version, from his POV. He tells it like it is, straightforward and to the point.<br><br>Being inside Drew's head and getting the entire story from his point of view, is one of things I loved most about this book. Some of his thoughts literally made me laugh out loud -<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The first is: God hates me. The second is: I have been a naughty, naughty boy for most of my life, and this is my payback. And you know what they say about payback, right? Yep. She's one hairy bitch."<br><br>**<br><br>"Edward Cullen can take his stupid heroine and OD on it. Kate is my own personal brand of Viagra."<br><br>**<br><br>"Would he open his bedroom door and let some other guy screw his wife? Okay, that was too far. I take it back - considering his wife is my mother. Forget I ever referred to my mother and screwing in the same sentence. That's just wrong...on so many levels."<br><br>**<br><br>"For God's sake, don't let her watch Cinderella. What kind of example is that? A mindless twit who can't even remember where she left her damn shoe, so she has to wait for some douchebag in thights to bring it to her? Give me a friggin break."<br><br>**<br><br>"Kate, if I throw myself in front of a bus,<br> will you come visit me at the hospital? <br> Drew<br>PS - try not to feel guilty if I don't survive. Really."</b>
</blockquote><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834273.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew Evens is a typical womanizer. Girls line the streets for him and he's never had to seduce a woman before.<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>"I've never seduced a woman before. Shocking, I know. Let me clarify, I've never <i>had</i> to seduce a woman before, not In the typical sense. Usually it takes a look, a wink, a smile. A friendly greeting, maybe a drink or two. After that, the only verbal exchange involves short one-word phrases like <i>harder, more, lower...</i>you get the point."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>But then he meets <b>Katherine {Kate} Brooks --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420533i/834274._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Drew meets Kate at a bar on a Saturday night, he's immediately drawn to her. She's beautiful and attractieve nu he's ready to make her his newest conquest for the night.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"She's magnificent - angelic - gorgeous. Pick a word, any fucking word. The bottom line is, for a moment, I forgot how to breathe."</b>
</blockquote><br>But Kate Brooks isn't the one night stand- kind of girl and when she turns him down, he can't seem to get her out of his head, because that's just something that's never happened to him before. Then, when it turns out, Kate is the new associate at his father's business company, the situation is about to get even more messier.<br><br>At first, Drew doesn't realize is yet, but Kate is the kind of girl that will turn his entire world upside down.<br><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834275.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not only can he <i>not</i> stop thinking about her, she's also become his new close co-worker and if there's one rule he's never, ever broken beofre, it's that he never mixes business with pleasure. But for Kate he might be prepared to make an exeption... <br><br></p><blockquote>
  <b>"Women fall in love quicker than men. Easier and more often. But when guys fall? We go down harder. And when things go bad? When it's not us who ends it? We don't get to walk away. We crawl."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>They finally give in to their attraction to each other and they do? Phew! The sex scenes from Drew's POV were just HOT!!! *fans self*<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409943ra/803174.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>Then Drew did some things that were just <i>not</i> okay...</b>
  <br>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834276.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>He messed up, badly <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and ended up breaking Kate's heart. Luckily, she has some good friends that are willing to bitch-slap him if ever burst her feelings like that again." <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br></b>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420533ra/834277.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When Drew tries to make things up with Kate, he goes all out, flowers, balloons, a music band...but Kate doesn't give in easily and I liked the fact that she stond up for herself like that instead of forgiving him right away. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But in the end, after some swoon-worthy Notebook-like attempts on Drew's behalf to make things right, the story does have a HEA.... *sigh*</b>
  <br>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413499ra/814257.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>There isn't one thing I didn't love about this book, from the dialogue to the main chracters and all the unique and funny side chracters like Alexandra aka "The Bitch", Mackenzie and Dee-Dee, I just enjoyed every minute of this fun, unique and hilarious story and ended up devouring it in one day...</b>
  <br>
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420534ra/834278.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</p></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_608623775" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608623775?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608623775" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7967510040346561291"><b>5+++ Fantastic and Hilarious Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/05086699-5eb3-4360-9bc5-06a87a0226bd_zpsb3c675a8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834544.jpg' alt=' photo 05086699-5eb3-4360-9bc5-06a87a0226bd_zpsb3c675a8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>If you are like me and you adore the lovable <b>assholes</b>, the<b> jerks</b>, and the<b> manwhores</b>... then <b>Drew Evans</b> is just the guy for you!!! This book had me hooked from the very first page and I couldn’t get enough! Being inside Drew Evan’s head was amazing! One of the funniest and most enjoyable stories I have read in a really long time! <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3f052d67-a57c-46ed-b442-d6c70f069a12_zps0c1e9fcf.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834545.jpg' alt=' photo 3f052d67-a57c-46ed-b442-d6c70f069a12_zps0c1e9fcf.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Meet Drew Evans. He is a successful business man, a handsome guy, he’s got great friends, a loving family, and as many women</span>
  <span id="freeText7967510040346561291" style="display:none"><b>5+++ Fantastic and Hilarious Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/05086699-5eb3-4360-9bc5-06a87a0226bd_zpsb3c675a8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834544.jpg" alt=" photo 05086699-5eb3-4360-9bc5-06a87a0226bd_zpsb3c675a8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you are like me and you adore the lovable <b>assholes</b>, the<b> jerks</b>, and the<b> manwhores</b>... then <b>Drew Evans</b> is just the guy for you!!! This book had me hooked from the very first page and I couldn’t get enough! Being inside Drew Evan’s head was amazing! One of the funniest and most enjoyable stories I have read in a really long time! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3f052d67-a57c-46ed-b442-d6c70f069a12_zps0c1e9fcf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834545.jpg" alt=" photo 3f052d67-a57c-46ed-b442-d6c70f069a12_zps0c1e9fcf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Meet Drew Evans. He is a successful business man, a handsome guy, he’s got great friends, a loving family, and as many women as he could ever want. Drew is hot and Drew knows it. Drew doesn’t do relationships. He never makes promises, he just does his thing. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1083348a-d2a3-41a7-8312-98574f46f73e_zpsa0bbe1e9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834546.jpg" alt=" photo 1083348a-d2a3-41a7-8312-98574f46f73e_zpsa0bbe1e9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Throughout this story, Drew gives us a ton of fun facts and info: <b>
  <blockquote>Men are visual. We wouldn’t be fucking you if we didn’t want to look at you. You can write that down.<br><br>I control my dick. My dick does not control me.<br><br>I sleep naked, by the way. You should try it. If you haven’t slept naked, you haven’t lived. But thats beside the point.<br><br>For those ladies out there who are listening, let me give you some free advice: If a guy who you just met at a club calls you<i> baby, sweetheart, angel </i>or any other generic endearment? Don’t make the mistake of thinking he’s so into you, he’s already thinking up pet names. It’s because he can’t or doesn’t care to remember your actual name.<br><br>Deep down- I’m a momma’s boy. I’m man enough to admit it. And trust me, I’m not the only one. Explains a lot, doesn’t it?<br><br>Here’s a fact for you – once I’m done, I’m done. I’m not the kind of guy who rides the same rollercoaster twice </blockquote>
</b><br>You get the idea of what kind of guy he is, yeah? Well, Drew hasn’t been himself. He has ‘the flu’. The last week he hasn’t been well. And it all has to do with one woman. <br><br>Katherine Brooks.<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/4a5fe392-1562-4b26-acd3-8cbc5b91e7b3_zps534371c7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834547.jpg" alt=" photo 4a5fe392-1562-4b26-acd3-8cbc5b91e7b3_zps534371c7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kate works with Drew. She is new at the firm and she is ready to succeed. She is smart, beautiful, feisty and she intrigues Drew in every way. There is something different about Kate. While competing against each other for the same account, these two bicker and banter back and forth... its hilarious! There is also some major sexual tension going on, but there are complications. They get to know each other better and Drew decides he wants Kate. Drew screws up a ton, but he is a guy, what do you expect? He goes through some great lengths to make it better. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3ea5a601-ee66-4690-9781-ac54cc89e9bf_zpsa161abd0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834548._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 3ea5a601-ee66-4690-9781-ac54cc89e9bf_zpsa161abd0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Some of the BEST lines:<br><b>
  <blockquote>It makes me want to kiss her and strangle her at the same time. I’ve never been into S&amp;M. But I’m beginning to see its benefits.<br><br>Edward Cullen can take his stupid heroine and OD on it. Kate is my own personal brand of Viagra.<br><br>Twelve days. Its a frigging record. I haven’t had a drought like this since the winter of ninety-nine. <br><br>“God! Oh God!” <br>“God’s not the one fucking you, baby.”<br>“Drew... Drew... yes... Drew!”<br><i>Much better.</i><br><br>“You have no sense of self-preservation, do you?” “No, not at the moment. I’m too focused on... fornication.”<br><br>I blame Adam. Now theres a guy who had the world by the balls. Walking around naked, a hot chick to satisfy his every whim. I sure hope that apple was tasty, ‘cause he really fucked it up for the rest of us.</blockquote>
</b><br>This is how I looked a majority of the book:<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/GIFS/LaughingGifes_zps4845fa54.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420584ra/834549.gif" alt=" photo LaughingGifes_zps4845fa54.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I can’t tell you how impressed I was with this debut novel! I don’t think I have ever read a book that has made me smile and laugh so much. I love the male pov and it was a treat to have the whole story written in the male’s pov! The whole time I was reading, I felt like Drew was talking to me. Drew is the best kind of character. He is funny, sarcastic, sexy and sweet! I couldn’t get enough of him! And I liked Kate too lol! The whole thing- It was great! Can I say there was <b>nothing</b> I didn’t like about this one! Loved everything it! Going on the favorites shelf for sure. Emma Chase- I will read ANYTHING you write lady! This was fantastic! Looking for a fun and awesome read... pick this one up!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/166216de-2a50-4a88-8944-56489cac5fee_zpsad231609.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420584i/834550.jpg" alt=" photo 166216de-2a50-4a88-8944-56489cac5fee_zpsad231609.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1077460358" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1077460358" />
    <a title="Anne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1720620-anne"><img alt="Anne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415374035p2/1720620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1077460358?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne" href="/user/show/1720620-anne">Anne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=recommended-by-a-not-stupid-friend">recommended-by-a-not-stupid-friend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=humor">humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=trashy-romance-novel">trashy-romance-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1077460358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13178637316112348985"><b>Douchebags, FTW!</b> <--reread 2017<br/>This one held up during a second reading, and I'd still recommend it to anyone who isn't looking for prince charming to actually be...charming.<br/><br/>Also.<br/>In the story, Drew is a brunette, but since the beauty of books is that I can imagine whatever the fuck I want... <br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495821427ra/22859079.gif' width='400' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Original review: 2014</b><br/><br/>LOVED THIS! LOVED IT!<br/>I laughed, and laughed, and laughed, and then I laughed some more. Sooooo good!<br/>I have to say that I understand why some people found this book (Drew's voice in part</span>
  <span id="freeText13178637316112348985" style="display:none"><b>Douchebags, FTW!</b> &lt;--reread 2017<br>This one held up during a second reading, and I'd still recommend it to anyone who isn't looking for prince charming to actually be...charming.<br><br>Also.<br>In the story, Drew is a brunette, but since the beauty of books is that I can imagine whatever the fuck I want... <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495821427ra/22859079.gif" width="400" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Original review: 2014</b><br><br>LOVED THIS! LOVED IT!<br>I laughed, and laughed, and laughed, and then I laughed some more. Sooooo good!<br>I have to say that I understand why some people found this book (Drew's voice in particular) offensive, rude, and obnoxious. He's a self-centered man-whore, and his inner thoughts are not even slightly redeeming. We first meet him while he's getting a BJ from a random redhead in a bathroom, and his immediate thoughts are only how quickly he can extract himself from her and move on to the next good time. <br>Because why in the world would he have sex with the same woman twice?<br><i>Hang on. Did she just say she had a twin? </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447002736ra/16942283.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Aaaaand we're back in business! </b><br><br>Is Drew honest, or is he just a horrible person? <br>Maybe a little bit of both.<br>Thing is, I married a guy who sounds like Drew. Many years later, I'm used to that particular brand of <i>honesty</i>, so it cracked me up on several different levels. <br>However, if you don't like leading men who aren't PC, then you'll want to steer clear of this one because this guy is guaranteed to offend you.<br>I get it, I do. It's just that my husband has used the excuse <b>
  <i>"because I'm not a giant vagina"</i>
</b> to get out of doing so many things with me that I'm desensitized to it.<br>At any rate, I loved Drew and Kate's story, and I can see myself coming back and revisiting this book over and over again.<br><br>This a typical romance in that Drew is unbelievably sexy, unbelievably rich, and unbelievably <i>skilled</i> with women.<br>I should be annoyed with his lack of Real-World issues, but this was funny enough that I managed to overlook his...<i>lack of flaws</i>, I guess? <b>Tangled</b> is one of those stories that I just chalked up to complete fantasy, and decided not to let my sensible side squish the fun.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496937825ra/22969844.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Mild Spoilers Ahead: </b><br><br>Here's what I thought the author did right:<br>First, when Drew realizes he's in love, he doesn't run off and deny it. <br>It doesn't make sense when they have characters do that, you know? If you're in love, you act the fool. You do the whole embarrassing PDA stuff, you talk about them until your friends want to strangle you, and you otherwise just act all goofy and stupid.<br>You don't run off. Not even relationship-shy dudes.<br>I think that's something certain people tell themselves when their love interest runs for the hills.<br><i>Oh, they're just scared of their feelings!</i><br>Ehhh. I think they just don't like you.<br>Maybe I'm wrong. <s>I'm not.</s><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496935940ra/22969605.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Second, it takes Kate a reasonable amount of convincing to take Drew back at the end.<br>I know that some of you are probably thinking she took him back too soon, but let's face it, she was crazy about him. If you already want to believe someone, then it doesn't usually take much for them to convince you of something. <br>She hung in there longer than I would have...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1495819208ra/22858859.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm not sure how I missed out on this little gem, but I'm sure glad I found it.<br>If you haven't read this one yet, you need to check it out!<br><br><i>
  <b>PS - You can thank <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/12618229-jeff" rel="nofollow noopener">Jeff</a> &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3461034-trish" rel="nofollow noopener">Trish</a> for all of the extra Hemsworth gifs I had sitting around...</b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13178637316112348985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer620934337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2807403208777991068"><br/><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395552ra/761882.gif' width='450' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Wrong!</i>
</b> It's Drew Evans.<br/><br/>Drew is crude, crass, vulgar. He's immature and spoilt. He wants only one thing from a woman. He's a chauvinist pig. He's a man whore. He is disgusting.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>He is hilarious!</i>
</b><br/><br/>Have you ever seen those romantic comedy movies where there's an undeniable attraction between the leads but they're also competitors in the office? This is the rom-com novel equivalent.<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422389i/840312._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For once this novel lives up to all the hype, squeeing and fangirling!<br/><br/>If you love romantic comedies, that</span>
  <span id="freeText2807403208777991068" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395552ra/761882.gif" width="450" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Wrong!</i>
</b> It's Drew Evans.<br><br>Drew is crude, crass, vulgar. He's immature and spoilt. He wants only one thing from a woman. He's a chauvinist pig. He's a man whore. He is disgusting.<br><br><b>
  <i>He is hilarious!</i>
</b><br><br>Have you ever seen those romantic comedy movies where there's an undeniable attraction between the leads but they're also competitors in the office? This is the rom-com novel equivalent.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422389i/840312._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For once this novel lives up to all the hype, squeeing and fangirling!<br><br>If you love romantic comedies, that are a bit on the....tasteless side, but <b>very</b> funny and <b>very</b> well-written, you will love <b>
  <i>Tangled!</i>
</b><br><br>I read this straight through without taking a break...for anything. I didn't take notes, I didn't highlight. So this review is....sparse. Take a gander at these gifs. It's all you need to know.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840313.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840314.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840315.gif" width="300" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840316.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840317.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840318.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840319.gif" width="300" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>And the good news is, Drew's got friends....</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422389ra/840320.gif" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final word.</b>......drop whatever you're reading, whatever you're doing.....and just read <b>
  <i>Tangled.</i>
</b> All right?<br><br><b>Steam:</b> 3.5<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1672004164" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1672004164" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1672004164?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Katerina by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/30934456">Τατιάνα Τζινιώλη</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1672004164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer484919811497757365"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Women fall in love quicker than men. Easier and more often. But when guys fall? We go down harder. And when things go bad? When it's not us who ends it? We don't get to walk away.<br/>We crawl.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>My hands have been itching to write a new review because, you know, it's more fun than highlighting the cases you have to know by heart. <s>(I will not cry I will not cry I will not cry)</s> So when God showed mercy and I could finally take a break and read a book before returning to the living hell know</span>
  <span id="freeText484919811497757365" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Women fall in love quicker than men. Easier and more often. But when guys fall? We go down harder. And when things go bad? When it's not us who ends it? We don't get to walk away.<br>We crawl.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>My hands have been itching to write a new review because, you know, it's more fun than highlighting the cases you have to know by heart. <s>(I will not cry I will not cry I will not cry)</s> So when God showed mercy and I could finally take a break and read a book before returning to the living hell known as Torts <s>(I will not cry I will not cry I will not cry)</s> I wanted something to cheer me up. Something <b>yummilicious</b>. <b>Smexy</b>. Something to leave me in the end <b>smiling</b> and <b>giggling</b> and <b>cursing</b> real life with its slim chances of finding Mr Perfect. <br>And <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_" title="Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a> was exactly what I needed!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402013518ra/9882484.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It makes me want to kiss her and strangle her at the same time. I’ve never been into S&amp;M. But I’m beginning to see its benefits.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Drew Evans is every girl's dream; successful, devilishly handsome and charming, he'll make you combust with one look and rip off your clothes (and his) with one touch. There's only one problem. The woman he can't get out of his head is rejecting him, and now they work in the same firm and they have to compete each other for a huge project. They fight, they share angry kisses and then they fight some more, until things happen and Drew gets the <i>flu</i> and he realizes that maybe his perfect life is not so perfect without Kate Brooks after all.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Because I had a life once. A life I loved. It was consistent. Fun. It was reliable. Safe. And then one night, a beautiful dark-haired girl came along and blew it all to kingdom come.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434126319ra/15177190.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's pretty accurate. Drew was <i>delicious</i>, his scenes with Kate were <i>delicious</i>, <i>
  <b>everything was delicious</b>
</i>! There's no female author that can write a male POV better than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6551005.Emma_Chase" title="Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Emma Chase</a>, she's the <b>I-know-what-men-think guru</b>! Is this a psychic thing? An otherworld ability? A pact with the devil? I don't know, but it's awesome! Given the situation between Drew and Kate and the reasons they could not be together at first, I'm not sure I would have enjoyed the story the same if it was narrated by Kate!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Newsflash, ladies: We can’t read your thoughts. And frankly, I’m not entirely sure I’d want to. The female mind is a scary place to be.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Drew could be a total <b>jackass</b> at some points, but he was a <b>funny</b> and <b>occasionally sweet</b> jackass. The way he talked to the readers, gave advice and commented on his story was extremely entertaining, it felt like there was a movie playing inside my head! And holy bananas! he was <b>
  <i>hot</i>
</b>. I was so dehydrated due to his hotness that I couldn't even drool. <br>I still can't.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466498812ra/19484957.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When you're in the mood for a book to cheer you up, read Emma Chase. When you're in the mood for a sweet yet hot love story, read Emma Chase. <b>Just read Emma Chase people!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="484919811497757365" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
