<div id="review_561741163" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561741163" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561741163?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=5-stars-read">5-stars-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=bookshelves-owned">bookshelves-owned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561741163" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13291817199142273630"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814171.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>I don't remember when was the last time I enjoyed any book so much. I laughed, I was entertained, I swooned. Tangled, book with witty and sarcastic hero as narrator, is a MUST READ! This insight into man's head and thinking is fascinating and a lot of fun.</b><br/><br/>My Drew and Kate:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814172._SY540_.jpg' width='250' height='340' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814173._SY540_.jpg' width='250' height='340' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW:<br/>Drew Evans used to be always on the top of things, getting everything he wanted and enjoying life of a single good-looking bachelor. Until he got flu which changed him into whinning man, lying down on his co</span>
  <span id="freeText13291817199142273630" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814171.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>I don't remember when was the last time I enjoyed any book so much. I laughed, I was entertained, I swooned. Tangled, book with witty and sarcastic hero as narrator, is a MUST READ! This insight into man's head and thinking is fascinating and a lot of fun.</b><br><br>My Drew and Kate:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814172._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814173._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW:<br>Drew Evans used to be always on the top of things, getting everything he wanted and enjoying life of a single good-looking bachelor. Until he got flu which changed him into whinning man, lying down on his couch and watching stupid movies for a whole week. Or was in not the flu that brought this strong man into this pathetic state?<br><br>After short prologue, story is set four months earlier to the times when Drew is successful gentleman who is enjoying services of various willing ladies every time opportunity arises. Yep, he is a man-whore. Also, Drew is extra confident person so when he meets woman he wants and cannot get, he is not willing to accept it. But what happens when proffesional competion and love gets into his way and complicates things? You get this superb and original romance story. <br><br>I loved "the voice" and style of writing in this book. It was magical, sarcastic, witty and funny. Perfection if you like to read something entertaining with well-thought storyline developement and sexy hero. I just completely adored Drew's inner thoughts and they were pretty hilarious too. I have never read about cockier hero than Drew Evans. But you will fall for him anyway, he is just that awesome. I personally will never forget him.<br><br>Kate was also awesome character. She was able to keep up with Drew all the time, matched his determination, even outsmarted him quite often. She was smart, gorgeous and ambitious. Dangerous combination when it comes to woman, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814174._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And story itself? It was flawless. There were moments that made me laugh, moments that left me all hot and bothered, as well as angsty or lovely moments. To be honest, I could not find single thing that I would not like about this book. <br><br>I hope this author will write more books in future. I will be reading it as soon as they come out. After reading Tangled, I am definitely her fan. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814175._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>* ARC provided by author as an exchange for honest review. *</i><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610081535?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610081535" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10507279636097417324">If I could give it more than 5 f*****g stars I would ...<br/><br/>I must say this was one of the most enjoyable books I have read this year. And that is saying something because I read a LOT! Marked this TBR before it’s release date when I saw someone review it.<br/><br/> I have been burned in the past by jumping on the bandwagon and “one-clicking” the books with all the rave reviews. So, I was a bit wary of downloading this on the first day, without reading some reviews from friends. I needn’t have worried. It was</span>
  <span id="freeText10507279636097417324" style="display:none">If I could give it more than 5 f*****g stars I would ...<br><br>I must say this was one of the most enjoyable books I have read this year. And that is saying something because I read a LOT! Marked this TBR before it’s release date when I saw someone review it.<br><br> I have been burned in the past by jumping on the bandwagon and “one-clicking” the books with all the rave reviews. So, I was a bit wary of downloading this on the first day, without reading some reviews from friends. I needn’t have worried. It was fantastic. It was brilliant. It was funny. It was sweet. You see, books can be written well, without resorting to smutty language, shock factor writing – yeah, ye know what I am talking about….. It is written from Drew’s POV, which is very original – OK, we have read books before with the Hero’s point of view but not necessarily the whole book, at least I don’t think so. I swear I laughed out loud so many times in this book. The review might be a bit long-winded as I felt I had to comment on everything. I could have highlighted something from every single page in this book, it was that good. It was pissing rain here this morning, Tuesday, I had to work, but as soon as I started reading this book, it felt as if the sun had broken through the clouds….. now I am starting to talk like Drew. Just sit back and enjoy this book. You will not be disappointed.<br><br><br>Drew, Drew, Drew, Drew, Drew … my new Book Boyfriend – yes I am a complete slut…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413478i/814172._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kate, Kate, Kate, Kate, Kate… my new Book Girlfriend … how she could put up with his Bullshit is beyond me …<br><br><br><br>Gotta love the cover for this book. If that does not inspire you to buy it, I’m not sure what will … maybe this review?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379792193i/560477._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Work colleagues thrown together …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118114.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, Drew, this says it all …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422217i/839744.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118115.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“I don’t care if you’re sixty, when a parent uses your full name, it pretty much sucks all the argument right out of you.”</b><br>- Tell me about it.<br><br><b> You’re a jerk.”<br>"You’re a ….an Alexandra."<br>"What the hell does that even mean?"<br>"Think about it. It will come to you."</b><br>- Still thinking about it – bit slow on the uptake here – don’t get it.<br><br><br>I like you, Drew...<br><br><b> No man wants to fuck a skeleton – and nibbling crackers and water like a prisoner of war at dinner isn’t attractive. It makes us think about what a cranky bitch you’re going to be later on because you’re starving.”</b> “<br><br><br><b>“That’s good, Kate. Fine. Love Billy. Marry Billy. Just please … God … please just fuck me.”</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835174.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> She whispers, “Fine.”<br>Fine’s a funny word, don’t you think? I don’t think there’s another like it in the English language that says so much while actually saying so little.<br>How many wives have told their husbands, “I’m fine,” when they really mean, “I want to cut your balls off with a butcher knife”?<br>How many men have told their girlfriends, “You look fine,” when they really mean, “You need to go back to the gym and work out – a lot.”<br>Its just the universal way of saying we’re just peachy – when we’re really anything but.</b><br><br>I really could keep adding quotes left, right and centre here, there are so many good ones…<br><br><br>Well done, Drew! Don’t think Daddy will be happy with you though!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835175._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you have read it, you will get this one ..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118116._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Look forward to hearing you eat your words, Drew..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118117.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> What’s that? Yes, I went to a Catholic school. You’re surprised? You shouldn’t be. My profanity has a certain religious flavor that can only be learned through a lifetime of Catholic education. <i>Jesus H. Christ .. Goddamn it … Jesus,Mary and Joseph… fucking. Christ Almight … holy fucking shit</i> - and that’s just what we heard from the priests. Don’t get me started on the nuns.</b><br><br>OMG, I fucking love it – so true – my language is dreadful so all I need to do is blame my fucking Catholic education and upbringing!!!<br><br><br>OK, now I “get” the “Alexandra” comment …. Took a while!<br><br><br><b>“We didn’t make it that far.”<br>“What do you mean?’<br>I smirk, remembering what an exhibitionist the girl had been.<br>“I mean that cab will never be the same again. And I think we scarred the driver for life.”<br>“You’re such a fucking dog, man.”<br>“Nah, I saved the doggie-style for when we were actually inside her apartment.”</b> <br><br><b>This moment will come back to bite me in the ass later on …</b><br><br><br>Even some of the stuff his friends say are hysterical …<br><br><b> Shifting into pick-up mode, Matthew replies,<br>“Delores is a gorgeous name, for a gorgeous girl. Plus it rhymes with <i>clitoris</i> … and I really know my way around them. Big fan.”</b> <br><br>Drew, you truly are a complete “Arse”<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835176._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah Jiminey “PISS OFF!”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118118._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>My, oh, My, that sex scene was smokin’<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380415925i/821314.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Predictably my cock springs up, like Dracula rising from his coffin… </b><br><br>I don’t know where she gets these lines from but they are great.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835177.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> I’ll never get tired of looking at her. Or kissing her. Pussy whipped, the name is Drew. Yeah I know. It’s okay. I don’t mind. ‘Cause if this is the Dark Side? Sign me up. Serioulsy. Don’t be surprised if I start skipping down the street singing, “Zip-a-Dee-Fucking-Doo-Dah.” I’m that happy.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835178._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> Fuck. Me.<br>No, that doesn’t quite cover it.<br>Fuck me with a chainsaw.<br>Yeah – that’s about right.<br>You ever see a singing asshole?<br>Here’s your chance:</b><br><br>Ah, Billy, you tried....<br><br><i>I was so blind I didn’t know<br>How much it would hurt to let you go<br>I want to heal us, want to mend<br>Come back, come back to me again</i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835179._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, Drew was really starting to draw me in and then he takes that phone call in front of Kate…. Seriously, Drew …<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379790963i/543961.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>DREW ….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118119.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aw, Drew, starting to like you again…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118120.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>…. And so it starts …<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118121.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118122.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I think these ones would have been more appropriate….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118123.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Every girl loves a gift in a little blue box..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> Sister Beatrice was a NILF! <br>I don’t need to spell that one out for you do I?<br>In those days, she was the youngest nun any of us had ever laid eyes on – unlike the bitter, black-robed hags who looked like they were old enough to have actually been around when Jesus was alive. <br>The fact that she was a woman of the cloth – forbidden – and in a position of power over us naughty Catholic boys just made it all that much more erotic.<br>She could’ve spanked me with a ruler any time.</b><br><br> OMG, Drew, you are going straight to Hell…..<br><br>“CPS” <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Chafed Penis Syndrome <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> – I LOVE IT!!<br><br><br><br>OK, OK, my pet peeve just happened….. aargggh – yes some of you know what it is, what annoys me more than the hero shouting “You’re Mine.”? Ye can’t remember – well, I’ll tell you what it is… a friggin Oirish accent. I’ll tell ye again, we don’t all talk like Darby O’Gill and the Little People! Or Tom Cruise in “Far and Away” … We do say “ye” for “you” sometimes, at least I do. So please all you non-Irish out there reading this, we do speak with normal accents, yes they are Irish accents but they are not “stage-Irish” accents.<br><br>Gotta love a Best Friend – you go Dee Dee!<br> <br><i>”So, I’m thinking you’re either a split personality caused by the raging syphilis coursing through your bloodstream – or you’ve got an itch for a good challenge. In either case, move along, jerk-off. Kate isn’t interested.”<br> <br>“I don’t know. Do you speak anything besides Asshole?”<br> <br>That doesn’t prove anything. Penises stick together.”</i><br> <br>She tells it like it is.<br> <br> <br>Great, Alexandra, his sister and Mackenzie (his cute niece) have just shown up… this should be good!<br> <br><u>Fuck fuck fuckity fuck.</u> - Yep, Drew, that is how you should be feeling.<br> <br> <br> <b>Closure is a made up word that women invented so they can overanalyze something and talk about it – to death. And then, after it’s been blessed and buried, closure gives them the excuse to dig the poor fucker up and talk about it – some more.<br>Guys don’t do that. Ever.<br>It’s over. Fade to black. The end.</b><br> <br> <br>Shame on you Drew, some of the best songs out there are in the Country Music genre..<br> <br> <b>I’m not really into country music, but Brad’s pretty cool. He’s a guy’s guy, even for a singer</b><br> <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZbGoK5RlD68">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZbGoK5...</a> <br> <br> <br><b>Besides, I like the word “fuck”. It implies a certain level of heat. Passion. And it’s specific. If Congress had asked Bill Clinton if he fucked Monica Lewinski, there wouldn’t have been any question about just the hell they were talking about, now would there?</b><br> <br> <br>Incredible…<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835180._SY540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118125._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>Now my life is a mess. In a good way. A giant unpredictable web of screw-ups and make-ups. Frustration and tenderness. Annoyance and affection. Lust and love. But that’s okay. Because as long as Kate Brooks is tangled up in that web with me?<br>Well, I can’t imagine anything fucking better than that.</b><br><br>EMMA CHASE .....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420797i/835181._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742952i/3118126.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.drewevans.net">http://www.drewevans.net</a><br><br>Emma Chase has a link on her website - FROM THE DESK OF DREW EVANS ... should be interesting.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer564711596" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9094382425584100212"><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/694/chasetangled1titlebysue.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413917i/815535.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/abs6bysb_zps3f0d5de5.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386265486ra/7325472.gif' alt=' photo abs6bysb_zps3f0d5de5.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★★! Tangled, book 1. Debut by Emma Chase. A hilariously witty tale following a non-committal playboy man-whore in his descent into the oblivion after falling for a girl he can’t have.</b><br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“My stomach flips with regret and disappointment. What I wouldn’t give for a time machine.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br/><u>Books/BONUS chapters in the Tangled series should be read in (this) order:</u><br/><b>Book 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/564711596' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tangled</a><br/>Book 1.1: <a href='http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/05/26/interview-with-drew-evans-from-tangled-plus-alternative-pov-from-kate-and-signed-paperback-of-tangled-by-emma-chase-to-be-won/#' rel='nofollow noopener'>Working Late/The Kiss</a></b> – Best read after chapter 6 of book 1. PLUS Interview with Drew.<br/><b>Book 1</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9094382425584100212" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/694/chasetangled1titlebysue.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413917i/815535.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/abs6bysb_zps3f0d5de5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386265486ra/7325472.gif" alt=" photo abs6bysb_zps3f0d5de5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★★! Tangled, book 1. Debut by Emma Chase. A hilariously witty tale following a non-committal playboy man-whore in his descent into the oblivion after falling for a girl he can’t have.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“My stomach flips with regret and disappointment. What I wouldn’t give for a time machine.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><u>Books/BONUS chapters in the Tangled series should be read in (this) order:</u><br><b>Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/564711596" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a><br>Book 1.1: <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/05/26/interview-with-drew-evans-from-tangled-plus-alternative-pov-from-kate-and-signed-paperback-of-tangled-by-emma-chase-to-be-won/#" rel="nofollow noopener">Working Late/The Kiss</a></b> – Best read after chapter 6 of book 1. PLUS Interview with Drew.<br><b>Book 1.2: <a href="http://www.emmachase.net/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bitch Strikes Back</a></b> – 1 month after book 1<br><b>Book 1.4: <a href="http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=14232" rel="nofollow noopener"> What a Difference A Year Makes: Exclusive sneak peek into the future Tangled </a></b> – 1 year later.<br><b>Book 1.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722046298" rel="nofollow noopener"> Holy Frigging Matrimony</a><br>Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/625149440" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted</a><br>Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722046315" rel="nofollow noopener">Tamed</a></b><br><br><b>Tangled</b> is just that a twisted, tangled tale about Drew and Kate, who met briefly in a bar only to, come Monday morning, discover that Kate is the new-hire at Drew’s Investment banking firm. Story is brilliantly told entirely from Drew’s POV and we get to follow him as he is thrown into what starts as an attempt at seducing a co-worker/sub-ordinate to a competition for an account and downhill from there…<br><br>I could go on and on about how much I enjoyed reading and stayed up all night to finish it. But <b>this story is best experienced.</b> As a matter of fact don’t even bother reading any further just hurry up and get your copy.<b>Thanks Ms. Chase for an entertaining , witty all-consuming read!</b><br><br>If you are <i>still</i> reading this, not heeding my advice, I have included my thoughts on Drew and Kate below plus some quotes to give you an idea of the wonderfulness that is Drew, droll playboy man-whore extraordinaire!<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“So that’s it. That’s my story. The rise. The fall. The end.” </b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/703/chasetangled1herobysueb.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413917i/815536.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Andrew Evans, Drew</b>, the prodigal son; spoiled, jaded and privileged, with uncanny good looks, smarts, wit and sarcasm, has at age twenty-eighth already made partner in his father’s boutique investment banking firm. He spends his weeks masterminding, structuring and closing deals affording him both wealth and industry respect. While his weekends are spent in careless pursuit of his next one-night stand, earning him a scandalous reputation and a never-ending line of potential conquests. That is until Kate! <br><br>Reading from Drew’s POV was truly a joy. Five words to describe Drew: <b>Sarcastic, witty, smart, insightful and unforgettable.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I tell them how it is, give them a good time and then the cab fare home. Thank you, good night. Don’t call me, ’cause I sure as shit won’t be calling you.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Newsflash, ladies: We can’t read your thoughts. And frankly, I’m not entirely sure I’d want to. The female mind is a scary place to be.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/694/chasetangled1heroinebys.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413917i/815537.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After meeting and getting to know Drew it was a pleasure to meet <b>Katherine Brooks, Kate</b> the woman who brought him to his knees or should I say sick-bed. From ordinary rather humble beginnings her intelligence, determination and ambition earned her a scholarship and a MBA at Wharton school of business. Upon her graduation she is hired by the prestigious <u>Evans</u>, Reinhart and Fisher. Her new job will prove challenging on so many levels much thanks to Drew. Not helping matters; she has also brought with her, to the big city, her high-school sweetheart and fiancé. <br><br>Five words to describe Kate: <b>Smart, beautiful, assertive, classy and loyal.</b><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I’m Drew, by the way.” I hold out my hand. “And you are?” <br>She holds up her hand. “Engaged.” </b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>And so their roller-coaster story begins; For Drew mostly a descent as his life spins out of control:<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“Although my mind recognizes that Kate Brooks is now my rival, apparently my c~ck hasn’t gotten the memo.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b> “I told you how I grew up. I never had to share my toys; I don’t plan on sharing my clients. Ask any four-year-old—sharing sucks.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I’ve gone cold turkey. Completely. I haven’t even jerked off. Not once. In nine frigging days. I think the buildup of semen is starting to affect my brain. Like sugar to a diabetic.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5+ stars <br>Heroine rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5+ stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 5 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 5+ stars<br><br>Would I recommend this series: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this series: Yes!!!<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/tumblr_lw0i0sbctO1r68no5o1_500_zps924d03fb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a></span>
  <span id="freeText16370399585955267688" style="display:none"><b> TWO STARS </b> <br>Tangled By <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6551005.Emma_Chase" rel="nofollow noopener"> Emma Chase </a><br><br><b>Genres:</b> Comedy/Erotica/Contemporary Romance<br><br>Kindle Edition, 254 pages<br>Published May 20th 2013 by Omnific Publishing<br><br>~**~~**~**~~~**~~**~**~~*~**~~**~**~~*~**~~*<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=qnpeo9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420878i/835461.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=331pu1t" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420878ra/835462.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Calm down you idiot! it is not about you!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=dc3go4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420878ra/835463.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>you should be happy that you are not involved in this disaster!! <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=34yxpaq" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420878ra/835464.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>this book was so bad, i just want to break the damn tablet, but i like my tablet so i suck it up for its sake!<br>EVERYONE is reading this book, so i said what the hell lets read it....<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=30bcvah" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420878ra/835465.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The fact that almost everyone gave this book 4-5 stars is absolutely ridiculous! The so-called "comedy" was SO forced the entire book. Now you will tell me that it was SUPPOSE to be sarcastic and funny, and that fact that it is from Guy POV play huge part in this. <br>I'll tell you darling this is bullshit!<br>First of all, if you know me you'll know that i LOVE books with boy POV , meaning i read a lot of those, this one was THE WORST!!!<br>And that is NOT a comedy! if you think so, then your sense of humor is dead .I'm sorry for your lost!<br><br>Some Authors can write HILARIOUS books and you feel that they come naturally. A high school student can write this before even taking writing 101. <br>Sad... <br>Don't get me wrong the idea behind this book is funny and brilliant, but the most important thing here is how to turn this idea to an actual <br>book! <br>YOU FAILED MY FRIEND.<br><br>I tried, i honestly tried to like it, like everyone else seems to, but i couldn't. I would read something and say hahah this is Fuu, funn,<br>no this is not funny!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=33kyv7a" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420878ra/835466.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Maybe it's me, maybe i don't have a sense of humor?<br> NAAAH i have an excellent taste and this book is rubbish.<br><br><br>Don't get me wrong, there are things that i liked, or i wouldn't give this two whole stars, for instance:<br>The relationship between <b>Drew Evans</b> and his niece. ADORABLE<br><b> Mackenzie </b> -the niece is adorable little girl , and i loved each scene she was in. And that what kept me going through the book. <br><br>There was some "wisdom" that Drew gave as a guy to women which i found helpful. To women out there which disparately -in my opinion they need to know about men and how they think:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If a guy who you just met at a club calls you baby, sweetheart, angel,<br>or any other generic endearment? Don’t make the mistake of thinking he’s so<br>into you, he’s already thinking up pet names.<br>It’s because he can’t or doesn’t care to remember your actual name."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>If he pees on you then he likes you!... stupid boys!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Sally Jansen.”<br>I look at him blankly.<br>Who?<br>“Sally Jansen,” he says again, then clarifies, “Third grade.”<br>The picture of a small girl with light brown pigtails and thick glasses<br>comes to mind.<br>I nod. “What about her?”<br>“She was the first girl I ever loved.”<br>Wait. What?<br>“Didn’t you used to call her Smelly Sally?”<br>“Yes.” He nods solemnly. “Yes, I did. And I loved her.”<br>Still confused.<br>“Didn’t you get, like, the entire third grade to call her Smelly Sally?”<br>He nods again and, trying to sound sage, says, “Love makes you do some<br>stupid shit.”<br>I guess so, because…<br>“Didn’t she have to leave early twice a week to go to a therapist because<br>you ragged on her so much?”<br>He ponders this a moment. “Yes, that’s true. You know, there’s a fine<br>line between love and hate, Drew.”<br>“And didn’t Sally Jansen switch schools later that year because—”<br>“Look, the point here, man, is that I liked the girl. Loved her. I thought<br>she was awesome. But I couldn’t deal with those feelings. I didn’t know how<br>to express them the right way.”<br>Matthew’s not usually this in touch with his feminine side.<br>“So you picked on her instead?” I ask.<br>“Sadly, yes.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br> Probbaly the best thing that has been said in this book. Sad i know!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Just so you know, men don’t expect a woman to smell like Winter Pine<br>or Niagara Falls or whatever the fuck those feminine products say. It’s a pussy—it’s supposed to smell like one. That’s the fucking turn on."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br> <br>I grew some respect for him here:<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Actions win wars. Actions heal wounds. Not words. Words are cheap.<br>Mine, in particular, have the combined value of pocket lint at the moment."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><br>~**~~**~**~~~**~~**~**~~*~**~~**~**~~*~**~~*<br><br>That's about it, I'm going to go, make myself a nice cup of tea and start reading a new book which actually WORTH reading. <br>Do i recommend this book to yu?<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=97796b" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1690634293" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1690634293" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1690634293?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=office-romance">office-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=i-laughed-hard">i-laughed-hard</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=damn-this-guy-is-perfect">damn-this-guy-is-perfect</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1690634293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18362636552298580064"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468374503i/19697835._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='190' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>5 Hilarious Stars!</b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>NEW BOOK BOYFRIEND ALERT</b>
</u>: <b>Drew <i>frigging</i> Evans</b><br/><br/>Why it took me so long to read this book is beyond me. If there's a guilty-pleasure New Adult book that is worth your attention, it's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_' title='Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tangled</a> by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6551005.Emma_Chase' title='Emma Chase' rel='nofollow noopener'>Emma Chase</a>. It's funny as hell and so addictive. Emma's writing was also so delicious you just can't get enough of it!<br/><br/>The story centers around <b>Drew Evans</b>. It's told in his POV. Yes, guys. His and his POV alone. I don't normally encounter a romance book where the only one that speaks is t</span>
  <span id="freeText18362636552298580064" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1468374503i/19697835._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>5 Hilarious Stars!</b><br><br><u>
  <b>NEW BOOK BOYFRIEND ALERT</b>
</u>: <b>Drew <i>frigging</i> Evans</b><br><br>Why it took me so long to read this book is beyond me. If there's a guilty-pleasure New Adult book that is worth your attention, it's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_" title="Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6551005.Emma_Chase" title="Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Emma Chase</a>. It's funny as hell and so addictive. Emma's writing was also so delicious you just can't get enough of it!<br><br>The story centers around <b>Drew Evans</b>. It's told in his POV. Yes, guys. His and his POV alone. I don't normally encounter a romance book where the only one that speaks is the guy. It's fun and refreshing in a way. It's nice to know Drew's thoughts-- including the dirty and naughty ones. lol. <br><br>So one night, Drew met this alluring brunette named <b>Katherine 'Kate' Brooks</b> in a club and yes, there was insta-lust in Drew's side (in a not-annoying way, mind you). Since then, he was not able to take Kate off his mind. And surprise! He learned one day that Kate's going to be his new co-worker in the company he's working which is owned by his dad. Now I won't get that far into describing the plot. Let Drew do the talking. Listen to him and prepare yourself for a bunch of laugh-out-loud moments because you'll surely get them here... all the freaking time!<br><br>Picture me while I was reading this<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468052787ra/19660278.gif" width="380" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443204759ra/16332752.gif" width="250" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You might think that this book only features tons of craziness and sexual nothings. Not. I learned a lot of things from Drew. His relationship tips are so sensible, I tell you guys. You want relationship facts and tips from the playboy's perspective? Drop your Cosmopolitan and listen to Drew.<br><br>As a sample, <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Assume nothing. Even if you think you know everything. Even if you're sure that you're right. Get confirmation. That whole "ass" cliché about assuming? It's right on the money. And if you're not careful, it could end costing you the best thing that's ever happen to you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Women fall in love quicker than men. Easier and more often. But when guys fall? We go down harder. And when things go bad? When it's not us who ends it? We don't get to walk away. We crawl."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>... and so much more.<br><br>What also entertained me most was Drew's set of analogies and comparisons that he added in almost everything that he narrated in this book, like:<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"She's like a Rubik's Cube. So frustrating at times that you want to toss it out the goddamn window. But you don't. You can't. You're compelled to keep playing with it until you figure it out."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>There were no dull moments in this book. What it offered was <b>pure entertainment</b>. My favorite scene and the one that definitely had me cracking up was the dinner scene where Drew's little niece <b>Mackenzie</b> talked and spoke a vulgar word that had everyone immediately react in such a funny way. (Drew's dad choking, Matthew spitting up the juice right on Steven's face, etc.) LMAO. I laughed for about three minutes with that! Also, I didn't only admire Drew and Kate's characters but I also adored the secondary ones, especially <b>Delores a.k.a. Deedee</b>. She's one badass woman and I can't wait to read her story and Matthew's.<br><br>This book also built up a remarkable sexual tension which led to sexual frustration and then some. Basically, the <b>relationship and character development</b> was amazing here. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18297707.Tangled__Tangled___1_" title="Tangled (Tangled, #1) by Emma Chase" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled</a>, as a whole, was a very entertaining rom-com book. It came packed with sizzling hot chemistry between the characters and it's simply designed to make you feel good and happy. I totally enjoyed Drew's POV here. The best! The ending was also wholly satisfying and it left me with a big smile on my face. This was my first Emma Chase book and it certainly won't be the last.<br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464648592i/19260109.png" width="250" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_609503990" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/609503990" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/609503990?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609503990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16875431195706578748">5 TANGLED DREW & KATE STARS<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420710i/834876._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='460' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I just hopped off the Drew Evans express and Well what can I say? first things bloody first, WHAT.A.RIDE. I didn't want to get off ... I unabashedly fell for Drew and Kate. <br/><br/>With that being said, Stop everything, drop everything and forget the following: food, housework, husbands, boyfriends, significant other, pets, social life, sleeping, etc. and READ.THIS.BOOK get your comfy spot, your kindle and dive right in.<br/><br/>I've got a total soft spot for a well put together book f</span>
  <span id="freeText16875431195706578748" style="display:none">5 TANGLED DREW &amp; KATE STARS<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420710i/834876._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just hopped off the Drew Evans express and Well what can I say? first things bloody first, WHAT.A.RIDE. I didn't want to get off ... I unabashedly fell for Drew and Kate. <br><br>With that being said, Stop everything, drop everything and forget the following: food, housework, husbands, boyfriends, significant other, pets, social life, sleeping, etc. and READ.THIS.BOOK get your comfy spot, your kindle and dive right in.<br><br>I've got a total soft spot for a well put together book from the Male point of view. Judging from the front cover of this novel who wouldn't want to get into this males head. This story is completely Refreshing, Outrageously Funny and utterly Lovely, lovely, lovely and yes I enjoyed the verbal foreplay just as much, if not more than these fictional characters.<br><br>The author sums up this book by her very own words right around 59% mark:<br><br>"The dashing playboy meets the take-no-prisoners girl of his dreams, and she snags his heart forever."<br><br>You know the drill ~ he's a man whore, she's the sweetest thing to have graced a books pages. They flirt, they fall out, they can't imagine life without each other blah blah blah ...<br>No STOP, Its more than that, MUCH MORE. I mean it is all of the above, but written so fabulously that you will be hooked. It is Full of heart, comedy gold standard funny and at the same time Devilishly naughty.<br><br>She's his curveball 'The one'. He's the epitome of 'allergic to commitment twenty something' add to the mix that they come together in a showdown of all office wars and you get ~'Tangled'.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420710i/834877._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420710i/834878._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This brilliant author has written a book with an air of confidence and originality and I'm pretty convinced I'll stalk this author for future releases. With all of that being said Starting this book I originally felt as though I missed a female voice - yes I'm well aware that the male point of view was a selling point for the story and believe me I was sold too, so after a while I told myself to get over it and enjoy the Drew ride and i did! call me crazy (I'm well aware of that fact) But I have a book butterfly radar, you know the effect of a book stealing your book sanity, the swoons, heart thumping that 'feeling'? well that was missing for me in some ways, but the brilliance of this laugh out loud, fabulously witty book more than compensated and as I got to the end of the book I sat back with a huge smile on my face thinking I understand the hype ~ I.TOTALLY.GET.IT.<br><br>Standing ovation for this authors debut novel, here's a few of my favourite quotes (the whole book could be highlighted).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420710i/834879._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❤❤“Edward Cullen can take his stupid heroine and OD on it. Kate is my own personal brand of Viagra.” <br><br>❤❤“Newsflash, ladies: We can’t read your thoughts. And frankly, I’m not entirely sure I’d want to. The female mind is a scary place to be.” <br><br>❤❤“My mother always told me, “Anyone worth doing, is worth doing well.” Okay, she didn’t actually say those exact words, but you get the picture.” <br><br>Last words from me, this book is stunning, funny, brilliant, sarcastic, touching, amazing, fan- bloody-tastic, but don't take my word for it ... Read on beauties, read on.<br><br>5 Drew Evans and Kate Brooks forever stars.</span>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">anyone with a sense of humor!</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer620637054" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15155374437849319952"><b>5+++++ HILARIOUS DEBUT STARS! Cheers for Emma Chase!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&current=genius_zps33365a5b.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>The stuff Drew would say.....<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/Spitting%20gifs' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br/><br/>My Drew- <br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps34c07d8a.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Drew Evans, egotistical, hilariously funny man-whore comes across a smokin' hot brunette </span>
  <span id="freeText15155374437849319952" style="display:none"><b>5+++++ HILARIOUS DEBUT STARS! Cheers for Emma Chase!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=genius_zps33365a5b.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>This entire book, I was like laughing my ass off. Seriously, full on asthma attack here people! This book is detrimental to your health. It should come with a WARNING -if you've got respiratory issues, a weak heart, just had a baby, had recent surgery- it'll seriously rip you the hell open! <br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/Laughing%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422344ra/840166.gif" alt="Laughing gifs photo: laughing tumblr_lr4f4onWrI1qk70fz.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The stuff Drew would say.....<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/Spitting%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>My Drew- <br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps34c07d8a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422344i/840167._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps34c07d8a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Drew Evans, egotistical, hilariously funny man-whore comes across a smokin' hot brunette in a bar. Time to turn on his charms- no woman can resist him. Oddly enough, this one does. And he can't get her out of his head. No worries as she's the new employee at his investment firm. Lovely. He doesn't "shit where he eats." No problem...he can resist Kate. No problem.....<br><br>My Kate-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps5ef3887b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422344i/840168._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps5ef3887b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Katherine is beautiful, engaged to her high school sweetheart, and just got her dream job. When she meets this uber sexy guy in a bar while celebrating her job, she's surprised to find out he's the owner's son....but she doesn't let on. She just discreetly turns him down.<br><br>My entire review could be filled with Drew quotes. The entire book is his voice, as he's speaking to you, the reader. I loved that idea. We get a lot of first person POV in books, but this was different. When an author can throw something new and different into a genre that's saturated with sexy alpha males and make it as enjoyable as this read, it's a sure hit! <br><br>I laughed throughout the entire book. I found myself quoting Drew to anybody that would listen to me. I guess they don't get it....Drew has to be experienced. Bravo Emma Chase. Your debut book is all the buzz and it's well deserved. I'll finish with just a few (hard to pick) quotes that made me laugh. <br><br>By the way, Drew's niece Mackenzie deserves a huge shout out! Loved her! She's Drew's little sweetheart. She's got a mind like a steel trap and is a star of the show! I'll start with her....<br><br><b>Mackenzie raises her hand proudly. " I have a bagina."<br> I smirk. "Yes, yes you do sweetheart. And someday it's gonna help you rule the world." <br>"Johnny Fingers has a penis. He say his penis is better than my bagina."<br> "Johnny Fingers is an idiot. Vaginas beat penises every time. They're like kryptonite. Penises are defenseless against them."</b><br><br>And another goodie-<br><b>The jar? It was invented by my sister, who apparently thinks my language is too harsh for her offspring. It's the Bad Word Jar. Every time someone- usually me- swears, they have to pay a dollar. At this rate, that thing is going to put Mackenzie through college.</b><br><br>Then there's Drew's buddy Matthew and Kate's friend Dee Dee. Please please please give us their own book!-<br><br><b>“Delores is a gorgeous name, for a gorgeous girl. Plus it rhymes with clitoris … and I really know my way around them. Big fan.”</b><br><br>Ah, but our dearest Drew succumbs to "The Flu." This has never happened to him. Can he survive it? It'll be a struggle for sure......<br><br><b>"I'm going to make you so happy Drew Evans." <br>My arms tighten around her. "You already have. After this? Heaven's going to be a major disappointment."</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15155374437849319952" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_865013354" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/865013354" />
    <a title="Mir" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/237469-mir"><img alt="Mir" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1275489063p2/237469.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/865013354?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mir" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mir" href="/user/show/237469-mir">Mir</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781476761770" href="/book/show/18404884-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer865013354" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14286088780743674170">Oh, I see why romance novels are so rarely written from the point of view of the male love interest: because men are revolting, objectifying, self-centered, manipulative, potty-mouthed assholes. <br/><br/>Chase isn't a bad writer -- she's lively, anyway, and her narrator's voice is fairly consistent, except when she tries to insert the occasional sensitive or politically correct sentiment -- but I sincerely hope men aren't all as awful as she imagines them. <br/><br/>If it were possible I'd add half a star for havi</span>
  <span id="freeText14286088780743674170" style="display:none">Oh, I see why romance novels are so rarely written from the point of view of the male love interest: because men are revolting, objectifying, self-centered, manipulative, potty-mouthed assholes. <br /><br />Chase isn't a bad writer -- she's lively, anyway, and her narrator's voice is fairly consistent, except when she tries to insert the occasional sensitive or politically correct sentiment -- but I sincerely hope men aren't all as awful as she imagines them. <br /><br />If it were possible I'd add half a star for having that rare beast, a woman who is actually good at her job (as opposed to the reader being informed that the woman is good at her job while she manifestly demonstrates otherwise). And moreover, good at a job that is competitive and ambitious and puts her into conflict with men. The lawsuit-worthy sexual harassment she puts up with at work is probably realistic, if the opposite of romantic. <br /><br />Nothing in this book was romantic to me. The "hero" was a manipulative, spoiled slut, and even when he decided he was in love with his coworker he never displayed any thought for her feelings, desires, or goals. Pressuring her constantly when she's just lost her fiance of ten years? Stalking and harassing her? Humiliating her in the workplace (which he gets away with because he's the boss's son) and preventing her from working effectively? Blackmailing her for a date? None of those were within the realm of acceptable human behavior to me, much less romantic. Oh, but he loves his four-year-old niece* -- awwww. He must be a sweetheart really.<br /><br />The most interesting thing about this book was its attempted intersection of male and female fantasies, although since the male perspective is mediated through the author's imagination of what men think like I'm not sure how useful that is. I preferred the two-author approach in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/225024.Don_t_Look_Down" title="Don't Look Down by Jennifer Crusie" rel="nofollow noopener">Don't Look Down</a>, where the man and woman were written by different authors. <br /><br /><br />*But not enough to refrain from having inappropriate and foul-mouthed sexual discussions in front of her.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14286088780743674170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

So I'll keep it sweet and short. <br><br>I am going to embarrass myself confessing this: I have writing that stupid thing down like a thousand times as in Rosalinda + [insert a random name here] forever.<br><br>Ok, embarrassment over, I must say I loved this book! <span id="freeTextContainer9290016396791902356">Alright ladies, see that amazingly sexy guy over there? Yep, that's the one, the hot one getting a blow job in the bathroom of a super trendy club<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422274i/839898._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Meet Drew Evans, God's gift to women!<br/><br/>Drew is a smooth talking, sexy, successful, man slut. Did I also happen to mention that he's a grade-A asshole? No? Well that's ok, because he's an honest one. He just calls it like he sees it.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>For those ladies out there who are listening, let me give you some free advice: If a guy who you just met at a club calls</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText9290016396791902356" style="display:none">Alright ladies, see that amazingly sexy guy over there? Yep, that's the one, the hot one getting a blow job in the bathroom of a super trendy club<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422274i/839898._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Meet Drew Evans, God's gift to women!<br><br>Drew is a smooth talking, sexy, successful, man slut. Did I also happen to mention that he's a grade-A asshole? No? Well that's ok, because he's an honest one. He just calls it like he sees it.<br><blockquote>
  <b>For those ladies out there who are listening, let me give you some free advice: If a guy who you just met at a club calls you baby, sweetheart, angel, or any other generic endearment? Don’t make the mistake of thinking he’s so into you, he’s already thinking up pet names. It’s because he can’t or doesn’t care to remember your actual name.</b>
</blockquote><br>I mean, you can't fault a guy for his honesty, right? He does pretty much lay it all for you.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Don’t look at me like that. I’m not a bad guy. I don’t lie; I don’t sandbag women with flowery words about a future together and love at first sight. I’m a straight shooter. I’m looking for a good time—for one night—and I tell them so. That’s better than ninety percent of the other guys in here, believe me. And most of the girls in here are looking for the same thing I am. Okay, maybe that’s not exactly true. But I can’t help it if they see me, fuck me, and suddenly want to bear my children. That’s not my problem.<br></b>
</blockquote><br>Well of course they do, Drew, you are a good looking, successful, and rich investment banker after all. Even old women have a thing for you<br><blockquote>
  <b>Old women have a thing for me. And I don’t mean a pinch-my-cheek, pat-me-on-the-head kind of thing. I mean a grab-my-ass, rub-my-junk, why-don’t-you-push-my-wheelchair-into-the-broom-closet-so-we-can-get-nasty kind of thing. It’s fucking disturbing.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422274ra/839899.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All women typically fall over themselves to sleep with you....right? That is until one brown haired, brown eyed beauty turns you down at a club.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422274i/839900.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Much to Drew's dismay, the gorgeous brunette that turns him down is actually Katherine Brooks, a new associate at his father's firm where Drew works. <br><br>When they are forced to work together to attain a new client for the firm, a competition wrapped up in sexual tension arises between the two. Who cares if Katherine has a fiance?! Drew knows what he wants<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422274ra/839901.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Without giving too much away, let me try to sum up what happens with a few choice quotes...<br><blockquote>
  <b>No, I haven’t fucked her. Not that I wouldn’t love to. Trust me, if she didn’t work for me, I’d hit that harder than Mohammed Ali.<br> ✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻<br><br>The way I see it, I could still go for the gold. Technically speaking, I didn’t meet Kate at work; I met her in a bar. That means she could forgo the label of “coworker” and retain the “random hook-up” status with which she was originally designated. What? I’m a businessman; it’s my job to find loopholes.<br> ✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻<br><br>As she starts to speak, my mind is suddenly filled with every hot-teacher fantasy I’ve ever had. They’re playing out in my mind right next to the ones about the seemingly sexually repressed librarian who’s really a leather-wearing, handcuff-bearing nymphomaniac.<br> ✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻<br><br>Then I flip Kate the finger. Immature, I know, but apparently we’re now both functioning at the preschool level, so I’m guessing it’s okay. Kate sneers at me. Then she mouths, You wish. Well—she’s got me there, now doesn’t she?<br> ✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻<br><br>"I can take a joke," she tells me, sounding insulted. <br>"Yeah? When?"<br>"When it’s not being delivered by a childish jackass who thinks he’s God’s gift to women." <br>"I am not childish."<br>God’s gift on the other hand? My record speaks for itself. <br>"Oh, bite me." I wish. <br>"Nice comeback, Kate. Very mature." <br>"You’re a jerk."<br>"You’re a…an Alexandra."<br> ✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻✻<br></b>
</blockquote><br><br>What follows the bickering is a whole lot of awesome and some major <b>STEAM</b><br><br>But then Drew has to go an ruin things with his big wounded male ego<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422274ra/839902.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But don't you worry, because what follows that is the grovel to beat all grovels<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/481696.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also <b>LOVED</b> Drew's relationship with his niece.<br><blockquote>
  <b><br>Mackenzie raises her hand proudly. “I have a bagina.” I smirk. “Yes, you do sweetheart. And someday, it’s gonna help you rule the world.” “Johnny Fitzgerald has a penis. He say his penis is better than my bagina.” “Johnny Fitzgerald’s an idiot. Vaginas beat penises every time. They’re like kryptonite. Penises are defenseless against them.”<br></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I could go on and on, but really, you need to read it for yourself to see how hilariously fantastic this books is. All I can tell you is this:<br><br>This book...it was<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/457144.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously! It was<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419512ra/831771.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Every time I read a new chapter, after I got done with my uncontrollable giggles (the good kind) I thought<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422274ra/839903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Emma Chase, I cannot believe this is your debut novel. Seriously woman<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/548470.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=quirky-funny">quirky-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer630960494" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10068356407048249975">Five stars is NOT enough to give this book. Ten stars wouldn't be enough. I loved, loved, loved Tangled. It was exactly what I needed to read right now. I am actually worried I won't be able to write something here to give it justice. Drew Evans is handsome, and knows it. He has women falling at his feet. And he doesn't believe in relationships. He never spends more than one night with a woman but always makes that night the best she has ever had. Then, he meets Katherine Brooks, Kate, and every</span>
  <span id="freeText10068356407048249975" style="display:none">Five stars is NOT enough to give this book. Ten stars wouldn't be enough. I loved, loved, loved Tangled. It was exactly what I needed to read right now. I am actually worried I won't be able to write something here to give it justice. Drew Evans is handsome, and knows it. He has women falling at his feet. And he doesn't believe in relationships. He never spends more than one night with a woman but always makes that night the best she has ever had. Then, he meets Katherine Brooks, Kate, and everything changes. She changes him, she is "the one!" Although it takes him awhile to figure that out. But, Kate is engaged to someone else, Billy. And, Kate works at Drew's firm and he has a strict rule that he does not date his co-workers. <br /><br />This book had me laughing out loud most of the way through. Drew is simply hilarious. The names he has for Billy go on and on. Drew has very colorful language, a hilarious way of expressing himself, most of which he says he learned in Catholic School. ha ha And most of which I can't bring myself to repeat. And, once he has finally admitted to himself that he is in love, the lengths he goes through to win Kate back are simply unbelievable. I just can't say how much I loved Drew and his antics. <br /><br />The entire book was told from Drew's POV. But, it was told in a different way than any other book I have read. It was told as if I was sitting in a room with Drew and he was telling the story. There are some pretty steamy sexual scenes in this book and plenty of bad language so it is most definitely for the over 18 crowd. I'm not sure if this is Emma Chase's first book or not but she hit it out of the park with this one and I cannot wait for the next book. Thank you Emma Chase for making my day yesterday spent with Drew and Kate the most fun I've had in a long time. I highly recommend this book. </span>
