<div id="review_620651816" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/620651816" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/620651816?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=hyped">hyped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=highly-rated">highly-rated</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer620651816" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13312644358008600020"><b>
  <blockquote>“Women fall in love quicker than men. Easier and more often. But when guys fall? We go down harder. And when things go bad? When it's not us who ends it? We don't get to walk away.<br/>We crawl.”</blockquote>
</b><br/>Okay, so I think I was the very last person of my friends to read this book...maybe the last in the world. I thought that I wasn't in the mood for funny. <br/><br/>Boy was I wrong.<br/><br/>I love an author who writes a story that I end up loving before I realize that I'm already halfway through the book. So if you're not in</span>
  <span id="freeText13312644358008600020" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Women fall in love quicker than men. Easier and more often. But when guys fall? We go down harder. And when things go bad? When it's not us who ends it? We don't get to walk away.<br>We crawl.”</blockquote>
</b><br>Okay, so I think I was the very last person of my friends to read this book...maybe the last in the world. I thought that I wasn't in the mood for funny. <br><br>Boy was I wrong.<br><br>I love an author who writes a story that I end up loving before I realize that I'm already halfway through the book. So if you're not in the mood for funny, don't worry. Drew will suck you in like you wouldn't believe. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422347i/840176.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There's NOTHING so great in a romance book for me than watching a proud man fall to his knees over a woman. Especially when the woman doesn't even try. This book encompasses so much of what I normally like, without caving to the tropes. Kate never tries to lure Drew in. She's just herself. No angst, no drama, NO GIGGLING, no coy glances and ridiculous flirtation. In fact, she actively tries to dissuade drew from page one. She's a confident career woman without being a bitch. But she also titillates the man whore Drew with no effort at all.<br><br>Poor Drew. It really is like he's hit over the head with a cinder block when he meets Kate...and he just doesn't understand what is happening. The two are sort of frenemies before they realize it, and their banter back and forth and then their actual recon missions to sabotage each other at work is nothing short of hilarious!!! I loved it, I loved it!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422347i/840177.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>And then there is the inevitable boinking...which, let me just say...was off the charts hot, and totally unexpected for me. <br><b>
  <blockquote>“God, she’s beautiful. I mean, look at her. She’s like a volcano going off—fierce and fiery and breathtaking. If she doesn’t find a way to ugly herself down, I’m going to be spending an awful lot of time pissing her off. Which might not be such a bad thing in the end. Angry sex is awesome.” </blockquote>
</b><br>Oh, and then....<br><br><b>
  <u>THE FALLOUT</u>
</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>“It’s simple guy logic: If a woman is angry? It means she cares. If you’re in a relationship and a chick can’t even be bothered to yell at you? You’re screwed. Indifference is a woman’s kiss of death. It’s the equivalent of a man not interested in sex. In either case—it’s over. You’re done.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>It's a doozy. Poor Drew. The stupid idiot. The stupid, stupid MAN!!!! And poor Kate. She tries so hard not to fall for the playboy. What IS it about playboys that gets us EVERY FREAKIN' TIME?!?! We all want to be the one who tames them. And Kate does it inadvertently. It's great to watch, because although this is touted as being hilarious and insightful, it's also very much a romance. Drew and Kate are both heartbroken. They love each other so much, and it's hard to watch them hurt each other because they are truly meant to be. Of course, the ending is a forgone conclusion, but it's still magic every time. Is that a sign of my simple mind? I don't really care. I loved this story! I loved Drew's point of view, his issues, his meldown, his love for his niece, his FLU! Gah! Just as everyone else, I fell for the playboy. Too bad he's Kate's.</span>

I swear!!<br/><br/>Its like Drew is telling us a story and what's even more impressive is when we get thoughts in our heads, Drew answers the question!!! It was like physically being WITH him!!<br/>Absolutely fcuking bril</span>
  <span id="freeText8748574938729899669" style="display:none"><br><br><b>I LoVED Loved LOVED this book!! </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839848.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where has this book been all my life?<br>I swear I was sitting with a huge GOOFY grin the entire book!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839849.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is no ordinary book. Its from a males POV! How refreshing!!<br>At times I wondered to myself, did a female really write this??<br>Emma Chase hit the nail on the head! I swear!!<br><br>Its like Drew is telling us a story and what's even more impressive is when we get thoughts in our heads, Drew answers the question!!! It was like physically being WITH him!!<br>Absolutely fcuking brilliant!!!<br><br>I didn't want the book to END!!! It was funny, goofy, romantic and had some of the funniest analogy's I've ever read!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839850.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Did I mention HOW MUCH I LOVED this??<br><br>Drew is gorgeous, intelligent, rich and oh so sexy!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839851.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew is a male Slut! And make no mistake his proud of it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839852.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is the type to sleep with different woman, in different ways (pun intended) and that's it.<br><br><b>"But here's a fact for you - once I'm done, I'm done. I'm not the kind of guy who rides the same rollercoaster twice" </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422258ra/839853.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Work came first, Always..<br>His only love is his family...<br><br>He likes it that way... Until Kate..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839854.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Yeah, I do have ‘ a thing’ for her. An extreme dislike of her. We can’t stand each other. She’s a pill. I wouldn’t fuck her with a ten-foot dildo.”"</b><br><br>But he doesn't like her right? HA!! who you kidding Drew??<br><br><b>"I don’t spar with Kate because I like her. I do it because her existence is screwing with the trajectory of my career. She’s a nuisance. A fly in my soup. A pain in my ass. As aching as that mother of a bee sting I got on my left cheek at summer camp when I was eleven."</b><br><br>She's everything he thought he never wanted or needed in his life.<br><br><b>"She tastes… Jesus , I’ve never done drugs, but I imagine this is what that first snort of cocaine feels like, that first shot of heroine. Goddamn addictive."</b><br><br>She turns his world upside down and takes over his every thought.<br><br>He wants her and he will have her.. Because Drew always gets what he wants... Always! <br><br><u>Problem: She has a douche bag waste of space boyfriend/fiancee.</u><br><br><b>"Why is Kate still with this loser? That’s the million-dollar question, kids. I’m not a snob. I don’t care if you pump gas or run the register at Mickey-fucking-D’s. If you’re a man, you work—you don’t leech off your girlfriend"</b><br><br>Hmmm..<br><br><u>Solution: Fcuk her and get her out his system and move on!</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839855.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Apparently, I’ve grown a conscience. I don’t know when it happened, I don’t know how it happened, but I am not happy about it"</b><br><br>Kate is resistant at first but one night she gives in to the sizzzzzzling chemistry they have!<br><br><u>Technicality: Drew falls in Love with Kate after an epiphany after sex...</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839856._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Edward Cullen can take his stupid heroin and OD on it. Kate is my own personal brand of Viagra."</b><br><br><u>Major FcuK Up:</u> Kate makes a choice and Drew assumes the worst resulting in him loosing her and being heartbroken for the first time ever---&gt; AKA The FLU<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839857.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now we see Drew fight for the woman he wants and loves and the plan of action<br>---&gt; Woo Kate and the rest of us in the process..<br><b>"She's magnificent - angelic - gorgeous. Pick a word, any fucking word. The bottom line is, for a moment, I forget how to breathe."<br><br>She's not just perfect - she's perfect for me." </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422258i/839858.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Oh what a sweet, loving, cheesy, sexy and sooo soo funny story! <br><br>Dammit this book is more than a 5star!<br>I don't think there are enough adjectives in the english language to describe how much I LOVED this!!<br></span>

<div id="review_608188156" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/608188156" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608188156?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016469942" href="/book/show/17951186-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608188156" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13307002722545320708"><b>ETA 7/7/13 ~ Bonus scene: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=14232'>http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=14232</a> ...you won't want to miss it...whips, Star Wars, Batman, Justin Bieber and the Notebook! </b><br/><br/><br/>4.5 ★'s<br/><br/>Straight up, Drew is a player...but he's a <i>straight forward</i> player. He lets his hookups know that he's only out for sex and usually for only one time. That is, until he meets Kate and his whole world is turned upside down. Come to find out not only is Kate engaged but she just started working for his company which is Drew's number one no-no</span>
  <span id="freeText13307002722545320708" style="display:none"><b>ETA 7/7/13 ~ Bonus scene: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=14232">http://thesubclubbooks.com/?p=14232</a> ...you won't want to miss it...whips, Star Wars, Batman, Justin Bieber and the Notebook! </b><br><br><br>4.5 ★'s<br><br>Straight up, Drew is a player...but he's a <i>straight forward</i> player. He lets his hookups know that he's only out for sex and usually for only one time. That is, until he meets Kate and his whole world is turned upside down. Come to find out not only is Kate engaged but she just started working for his company which is Drew's number one no-no.<br><br>This book is written from Drew's POV and the author has written it so he "talks" to the audience. Even though that's not new, I found it really refreshing and interesting and the things that Drew says are just downright hilarious! <br><br><b>
  <u>My Drew</u>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791776i/554709._SY540_.jpg" width="350 height=" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yummo, right? Yes...Drew is all that and he knows it and he's not shy about letting you know it. But he is in no way prepared for Kate and he is drawn to her like a moth to flame. He absolutely can not get her out of his mind and fortunately for him, it seems she feels the same way. <br><br>Kate is interesting and has quite a background...but she had me at her love for the perfect pillow! Since we're essentially having the shoe on the other foot now...we don't know a lot about what she is thinking. Oh, we get the passionate kisses but she is able to reign things in...for now. <br><br>Then, things happen in Kate's life and she's suddenly available. Drew tries to be a good boy and give her time especially after he walks in on her crying. <i>Poor guy can't even last a week!</i> But at least she did get some time! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791776i/554710.jpg" width="400 height=" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew and Kate together are wonderful, sweet and HOT!! Did I say hot?? W-O-W and lucky for us, the sex scenes are written by a woman because I'm not sure I could have handled them actually written by a man. <br><br>I think that's my only complaint...having Drew's POV, a male's POV, we miss out on a lot of those romantic things...the sweetness and the softness and instead we get a whole bunch of TESTOSTERONE! But there is a saving grace but I'll get to that in a minute. <br><br>Drew and Kate have a wonderful weekend but come Monday morning, something happens. And as usual for a man (no judgment here), Drew fears the worse and regresses to his earlier behavior causing him to come down with what he thinks is the FLU!! OMG...he is the biggest baby EVER...and I loved every moment of it! <br><br>Never fear...with the help of a great set of characters (his friends and family), Drew's able to pull out of his illness and tackle his problem head on. Many kudos to him...even if he went a bit overboard! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791776i/554711.jpg" width="400 height=" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would be remiss if I didn't talk about some of the other characters. Drew's friends are just as hilarious and while some are still players, others have settled down and/or are settling down. Matthew and Dee-Dee seem very interesting and I would love to read more about them and I even love Lexi and Steven! But my all time favorite character has to be Mackenzie! What an amazing character and I love her relationship with Drew. The cussing jar and the horse were hilarious! <br><br>And something else that plays almost as important part as the characters are all the movie references. From Cinderella to Ron Burgundy, Little Mermaid to The Notebook, I loved how EC incorporated it into many of the relationships....<i>just like real life!</i> <br><br>I loved the ending...Yay for no cliffhanger! And I think most people will be satisfied. I've heard a rumor that there may be a possible book two...that would be awesome! But until then, check out this link for a scene from Kate's POV: (thanks to my lovely friend, D Kristin!)<br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://asainandwhitegirlbookblog.wordpress.com/2013/05/24/blog-tour-tangled-by-emma-chase-review-giveaway-and-an-alternate-pov-from-kate-the-bitch-strikes-back/">http://asainandwhitegirlbookblog.word...</a><br><br>Want more Drew? The author has a website set up called <i>From the Desk of Drew Evans</i> that you can check for even more hilarity...and wisdom? ;) <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.drewevans.net/">http://www.drewevans.net/</a><br><br><br>Favorite quotes: (way too many to add them all!)<br><br>♦ "I know, I know…I said I don’t ride the same coaster twice. But twin coasters? <br><br>Let me tell you, no man would pass up a ride like that."<br><br>♦ "Maybe you’ll understand my point of view if I put it this way. You brush your teeth, right? Well, suppose your favorite toothpaste is Aquafresh. But the store is out. All they have is Colgate. What are you going to do? You’re going to use the Colgate, right? <br><br>You may want to brush with Aquafresh, but when all is said and done, you use what you have to keep those pearly whites clean. See my way of thinking? Good."<br><br>♥ I smile devilishly. “I’d love to eat your cookie, Kate.” <br><br>She shakes her head at me. “Why do I have the feeling you’re not talking about the chocolate chip variety?”<br><br>♦ "In times like this, I always ask myself, "What would William Wallace do?"<br><br>♥ “So I said those things on purpose, so you would think you were nothing to me. That you were just another girl. But you’re not, Kate. You’re not like anyone I’ve ever known. I want to be with you…really be with you. Only you. I’ve never felt this way about anyone. And I know I sound like a freaking Hallmark card, but it’s true. I’ve never wanted all the things I want to have when I’m with you.”<br><br>♦ “It’s the estrogen. It gives us ESP. If you had a vagina, you’d know too.”<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13307002722545320708" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_608163006" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/608163006" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608163006?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16073738-tangled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=sexy-suit-and-ties">sexy-suit-and-ties</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=fav-book-boyfriend">fav-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=lol-funny">lol-funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=meli-s-top-favourites">meli-s-top-favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608163006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2438499832468733358"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790308._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><b>***5 I CAN'T BREATHE, WIPING TEARS, STOMACH CRAMPING STARS***</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445450807ra/16652068.gif' width='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>OMG! I am SO glad I decided to see what all the fuss was about with this book. I FREAKING LOVED IT! Being in Drew's head was absolutely FUN and HILARIOUS! IT IS A MUST READ!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420516i/834202.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve never seduced a woman before.<br/>Shocking, I know.<br/>Let me clarify. I’ve never had to seduce a woman before, not in the typical sense. Usually it just takes a look, a wink, a smile. A friendly greeting, maybe a drink or two. After that, the only verbal exch</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText2438499832468733358" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405576i/790308._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>***5 I CAN'T BREATHE, WIPING TEARS, STOMACH CRAMPING STARS***</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445450807ra/16652068.gif" width="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>OMG! I am SO glad I decided to see what all the fuss was about with this book. I FREAKING LOVED IT! Being in Drew's head was absolutely FUN and HILARIOUS! IT IS A MUST READ!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420516i/834202.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve never seduced a woman before.<br>Shocking, I know.<br>Let me clarify. I’ve never had to seduce a woman before, not in the typical sense. Usually it just takes a look, a wink, a smile. A friendly greeting, maybe a drink or two. After that, the only verbal exchange involves short, one-word phrases like harder, more, lower… You get the point.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Drew is a <b>wealthy arrogant playboy</b> that is use to getting his way. He doesn't work to get a woman to sleep with him because he is so <b>handsome</b> and <b>charming</b> that women practically beg him to sleep with them. On a weekend out on the town, he sees a woman that he <b>needs</b> to know, Katherine Brooks. He wants her <b>bad</b> and isn't unsettled by the fact that Kate is engaged because her body language is <b>screaming</b> that she is very much <b>interested</b>. Still, Kate turns him down and he finds out the next day that she is his new co-worker and his father has asked him to take her under his wing. <b>Let the hilarious sexiness begin</b>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“…You and Kate. It’s obvious you have a thing for her.”<br><br>“Yeah I do have ‘a thing’ for her. An extreme dislike of her. We can’t stand each other. She’s a pill. I wouldn’t fuck her with a ten foot dildo.”<br>Okay that’s not true. I’d so fuck her. But I wouldn’t like it. <br>Yeah you’re right. That’s not true either.<br><br>++++++++++++++++++++<br><br>“She looks like some mythical imp, some fabled pagan sex deity from a Roman legend. Or a well-acted porno.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I <b>loved</b> Emma Chase's writing style. I was <b>hooked</b> just from the opening lines. It was all completely in Drew's POV and I could <b>not</b> get enough of reading all of the inner ramblings of Drew's mind. The things that came out of his head... some were <b>borderline</b> offensive but you can't help but think it's so <b>true</b>. You should see how much I highlighted this book! It was quite <b>refreshing</b> to read how <b>honest</b> he was. Obviously the inner workings of a woman's and man's mind differ but I <b>enjoyed</b> and was fascinated being in a man's mind. I didn't want it to end!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/492508.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drew was a bit of a <b>jerk</b> and <b>sarcastic</b>, but really <b>sexy</b> and in then end, you <b>really</b> can't say no to him. He was <b>irresistible</b> and <b>swoony</b>. <i>I want to have your babies! haha!</i> I loved how he started to change and was falling for Kate. He was a freaking idiot at one point, though. Still, <b>I LOVE YOU!!!</b> The way he was trying to make her fall in love with him had me sighing and laughing all at once. When he does something, he goes all out. I loved it!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420516i/834203._SX540_.jpg" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“God, she’s beautiful. I mean, look at her. She’s like a volcano going off—fierce and fiery and breathtaking. If she doesn’t find a way to ugly herself down, I’m going to be spending an awful lot of time pissing her off. Which might not be such a bad thing in the end. Angry sex is awesome.” <br><br>+++++++++++++++++<br><br>"Edward Cullen can take his stupid heroin and OD on it. Kate is my own personal brand of Viagra."<br><br>+++++++++++++++++<br><br>“She’s not just perfect – she’s perfect for me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I even really liked Kate. She was <b>intelligent, kind, fiesty, and sexy</b>. She was not afraid to be herself or work hard to get what she wants. I loved that she wanted to be independent because of how she grew up. My only complaint would be, <b>HOW COULD YOU NOT SAY YES TO HIM, YOU CRAZY WOMAN?!</b> Other wise, I think she kinda kicked ass.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If we’re going to work together, Drew, I think we should get a few things straight. I’m not your sweetheart. My name is Kate — Katherine. Use it. And I’m not a kiss-ass. I don’t have to be. My work speaks for itself.”<br><br>++++++++++++++++<br><br>“It makes me want to kiss her and strangle her at the same time. I’ve never been into S&amp;M, but I’m beginning to see its benefits.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445450807ra/16652069.gif" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In fact all the characters were very entertaining in their own way.<br><b>Mackenzie</b> - So freaking adorable with her little swear jar and the questions she would ask.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Uncle Drew?” <br>“Yes?” <br>“Is you gonna die alone?” <br>I smirk. “I don’t plan on dying for a long time, honey.” <br>“Momma says you gonna die alone. She tol’ Daddy that you gonna die and it be days till a cleanin’ lady find your rottin’ corpse.”<br><br>+++++++++++++++++<br><br>“I don’t think Uncle Matthew can come, Momma. He been too busy bein’ pussy whipped. Wha’s pussy whipped, Daddy?” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>"The Bitch" aka Alexandra</b>, his sister - Was supportive and mean all at once. She kind of reminded me of my relationship with my younger brother. So I thought that was brilliant.<br><br><b>Matthew</b> - He had a few hilarious lines that were really great.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Delores is a gorgeous name, for a gorgeous girl. Plus it rhymes with clitoris … and I really know my way around them. Big fan.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Seriously, <b>no</b> character got on my nerve. I also need to mention that the sex scenes in his POV, were also really good! <b>*fans self*</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445450807ra/16652070.gif" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I had so much fun reading this! I <b>laughed, giggled, snorted, rolled my eyes, sighed, swooned and smiled</b> so much my cheeks were hurting by the end of it. If you want a book that will <b>lift</b> up your spirts, <b>this is it!</b> It was so <b>AWESOME</b>!! I can't say enough about how much I <b>LOVED</b> it!! I am hoping that another book like this will be written by Emma Chase and hopefully coming out soon! *fingers crossed*<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Now my life is a mess. In a good way. A giant unpredictable web of screw-ups and make-ups. Frustration and tenderness. Annoyance and affection. Lust and love. But that’s okay. Because as long as Kate Brooks is tangled up in that web with me?<br>Well, I can’t imagine anything fucking better than that."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I'm not lying... the quotes could go on...<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="2438499832468733358" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DHLMzo1N6dJXg8TKk9f7uJcT7reBGnN0rgnx6VoBGnhL1A8BtPPWdc/NI7UVuMRbo3JY2xSTh6eHKwV45ciHnQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3t05gFwoA+094+/y5POFCuRciR/tEepRDrdPWELpkXqZe/pPZZY8SqWtCI1inLrp0D0/c3iYHoInlbvJ/SAMnw==')})
  }

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_15858248'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15858248-wallbanger?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Wallbanger (Cocktail, #1)<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/3379564.Alice_Clayton?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Alice Clayton<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.05 avg rating &mdash; 177,451 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2012\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer13096878462507159149\">The first night after Caroline moves into her fantastic new San Francisco apartment, she realizes she\'s gaining an intimate knowledge of her new neighbor\'s nocturnal adventures. Thanks to paper-thin walls and the guy\'s athletic prowess, she can hear <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText13096878462507159149\" style=\"display:none\">The first night after Caroline moves into her fantastic new San Francisco apartment, she realizes she\'s gaining an intimate knowledge of her new neighbor\'s nocturnal adventures. Thanks to paper-thin walls and the guy\'s athletic prowess, she can hear not just his bed banging against the wall but the ecstatic response of what seems (as loud night after loud night goes by) like an endless parade of women. And since Caroline is currently on a self-imposed dating hiatus, and her neighbor is clearly lethally attractive to women, she finds her fantasies keep her awake even longer than the noise. So when the wallbanging threatens to literally bounce her out of bed, Caroline, clad in sexual frustration and a pink baby-doll nightie, confronts Simon Parker, her heard-but-never-seen neighbor.
